He Bingxian Lectures on International Trade; Last Year's Trade Deficit Decreased Due to Weak Purchasing Power; Gu Jigao Says Trade Deficit is Not Absolutely Disadvantageous 142

The International Problems Research Association and the International Trade Association invited He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, to lecture on "International Trade Issues" at the Bank Club on Hong Kong Road at 5 PM yesterday. Members of the two associations, including Guo Bingwen, Li Zhaohuan, Chen Zheqing, Shen Xinqing, Cai Wuji, Gu Jigao, Xu Fengshi, Liu Shimu, Zhang Xianglin, Zhu Shaoping, and Tu Chuyu, attended. Mr. Weeks, editor of the American Asiatic Review, who happened to be traveling in Shanghai, was also invited to participate in the tea party, which was chaired by Li Zhaohuan. The following is a record of He's speech and the discussion. Reduced Trade Deficit.

Mr. He began by saying that the scope of international trade issues

is too broad to be covered in a short period of time. He will briefly describe the analysis of import and export trade last year and study the questions found in international trade statistics. The total import and export trade of the country last year was over 1.95 billion yuan, a decrease of 19% compared to the previous year (1932). The total amount of imports was over 1.3 billion taels, a decrease of 18% compared to the previous year.

The total amount of exports was over 610 million taels, a decrease of 20% compared to the previous year. However, this ratio of decrease cannot be used as a basis for research, because the import and export figures of the Northeast customs were included in the first half of the previous year. If the figures of the Northeast customs for the first half of the previous year are removed for comparison, then imports last year decreased slightly compared to the previous year, while exports increased by more than 40 million taels. Comparatively, the trade deficit decreased by more than 100 million taels. Weak Purchasing Power.

The reduced trade deficit is a good phenomenon at first glance, but if one considers the reality, the decrease in imports is actually due to the bankruptcy of China's rural areas and the weak purchasing power of the people. It is not optimistic because China has increased import taxes, while exports are still mostly raw materials. As for the classification of goods, the largest imports are agricultural products such as rice, wheat, and cotton, followed by new industrial products. Exports are mostly silk, tea, tung oil, etc., which have not changed slightly compared to decades ago.

Decrease with Japan. Observing by country, the United States ranks first in imports, the United Kingdom ranks second, Japan ranks third, and Germany ranks fourth. As for export countries, Hong Kong ranks first, the United States ranks second, and the United Kingdom and Japan rank next. This is different from the previous years, when Japan was the largest in both imports and exports. The reasons for this are certainly not limited to one, and the impact of the loss of the Northeast is perhaps the greatest.

Statistical Difficulties. When studying international trade, customs statistics are the most reliable basis. If it is extrapolated and compared with the statistics of other countries, there should logically be the same result. For example, if we have a trade deficit with them, then they must have a trade surplus with us. However, the results are unexpected. For example, China has had a trade deficit with Italy and Germany for many years, but the trade statistics of Italy and Germany show that they also have a trade deficit with China, which is a strange thing. The reasons for the discrepancy may be the following three points: First, the statistical methods are different. For example, due to re-export, China includes the country of the port of export, while other countries do not. Or, goods passing through Hong Kong are considered by them to be exported to Hong Kong, while we include them in the original exporting country. Second, the estimated prices of goods are different. Third, or there are still unreported tax imports.

This Year's Observations. After He finished his speech, Guo Bingwen and others successively expressed their opinions and briefly discussed how to balance international trade. Later, Gu Jigao asked He about the prospects for trade this year and whether there were any better hopes. He replied that it is not easy to collect sufficient materials to base on this time, so it is difficult to make a definite prediction. However, in his personal opinion, if silver prices continue to rise, the prospects for export trade are not optimistic.

Gu's Opinion. Next, silver expert Gu Jigao expressed his opinion on the trade deficit issue, saying that a trade deficit is not absolutely disadvantageous to us. For example, Japan and the United Kingdom are both trade deficit countries, but they are not weak because of it. In China, which has a backward industry, if domestic prices do not fall, then because of the higher interest rates, overseas Chinese and foreigners are happy to invest, so that the industry can be gradually built. The investors are not cash, but goods that are in trade deficit, so it does not have a very bad impact on us. Therefore, the trade deficit has increased in recent decades, but the outflow of cash is not much. After 1930, China increased tariffs, but the increase was not of a protective nature, but only to increase fiscal revenue. Afterwards, the world economic panic followed, creating a bad trade environment. In recent years, although the amount of imports in the customs trade books has increased, it is entirely due to the gold exchange rate relationship. In reality, we exchange a huge amount of agricultural products for a small number of goods from other countries. If you want to use artificial force to force a trade balance, it will inevitably lead to lower prices for agricultural products, forcing a huge amount of exports, which will further plunge the national economy into difficulty.

Tonghua Steamer Imported and Crashed Into a River Pontoon Lightship 148

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tonghua steamer returned to Shanghai from Shantou yesterday. When it reached the Jinliyuan Wharf in the Huangpu River, it crashed into a customs river pontoon lightship. Details are as follows:

There Was Fog En Route

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tonghua steamer last sailed from Shanghai fully loaded with cargo to Shantou. When it returned from Shantou to Shanghai, because most of the local cargo was loaded by the Taikoo and Jardine Matheson steamers, the Tonghua only carried 75 pieces. Returning to Shanghai was almost like traveling empty. The ship encountered heavy fog on the Zhejiang sea. The captain, Jiang Changqing, navigated very cautiously. Because he was traveling empty, he dared not take risks, so he anchored and waited for the fog to clear at Baijiemen. After a day and a night, when the fog cleared, he set sail, which delayed the voyage by one day. He only arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning.

Entering the Port and Anchoring

Yesterday, the Tonghua steamer entered the port. The Bureau was crowded with old and jointly transported goods waiting to be transported, so it ordered it to berth at the Jinliyuan Wharf in the South City in order to load cargo. The Tonghua steamed into the Huangpu River and went straight to the South Wharf. Lightly loaded and with fast currents, the captain ordered it to move slowly forward. When the Tonghua reached the river surface near the Xinjiangtian Wharf, it turned around as usual. At that time, the engine had stopped. After turning the hull straight, it docked at the Jinliyuan Wharf.

The Lightship Did Not Leave

In each section of the Huangpu River, the Jianghai Customs routinely dispatched a lightship at night to be stationed on the river pontoon, displaying lights to warn. At dawn, the lightship must be withdrawn. When the Tonghua arrived in front of River Pontoon No. 5 (that is, the Xinjiangtian Wharf river pontoon), it was already dawn, but the Shanghai Customs lightship on the river pontoon had not yet left. At that time, the Tonghua ship arrived and wanted to turn around urgently. The tide was also rapid. The lightship was obstructing the turn. The crew of the Tonghua shouted loudly to open quickly to avoid causing trouble.

The Hull Was Wrecked

At that time, there were three people on the lightship. They noticed that the Tonghua had arrived and were informed to cut the ropes and leave quickly. The people on the lightship did not pay attention. The Tonghua's engine did not start and took advantage of the tide to turn around. The lightship did not avoid it in time and was hit. The stern of the ship was sinking into the river. Fortunately, the three people in the lightship grabbed the river pontoon and were saved from falling into the water. However, the lightship had been wrecked. Fortunately, the Tonghua quickly retreated, otherwise River Pontoon No. 5 would also have been affected and destroyed.

The Ferry Towed It Away

After the customs lightship was wrecked, the ferry from Dongmen Road arrived and tried to tow the wrecked lightship to the South City. It also reported to the customs. After the Tonghua stopped, the captain, Jiang Changqing, also went to the head office and reported the details of the customs lightship obstructing navigation and being wrecked to the shipping department.

One thief was left to guard the gate, and the remaining three thieves entered the shop, each taking out a gun, and drove all the employees of the shop into the厢房of the Lisheng Sugar Warehouse in the third building. A robber wearing a black gabardine long gown stayed there and guarded the employees' actions with a gun. Two thieves then broke into the accounting room of the shop and the bedroom of Chen Lisheng, the owner of the Lisheng Sugar Warehouse, and rummaged through boxes and chests, looting a total of more than 2,000 yuan in banknotes from the shop's accounting table (of which 1,000 yuan were new banknotes from the Bank of Communications, and each banknote was stamped with the hidden mark "民". There were also 700 yuan of semi-new and old banknotes from the Central Bank, each of which was also stamped with the code "42". The rest were various banknotes.), 90 cents in small foreign currency, and jade bracelets, pearl bracelets, pearl hairpins, pearl ear picks, etc., each, stored in Chen Lisheng's family's boxes, and carried the stolen goods out the door. Together with the thief standing guard at the gate, they scattered and fled. However, the thief who was monitoring the employees had not yet realized that his accomplices had already obtained the stolen goods and fled, so he was still standing in the last building, yelling at the employees to keep quiet. As a result, one of the employees took the opportunity to sneak out of the shop and reported to police officer Duan Jingming of the nearby 13th post for assistance in the arrest. After hearing the report, the police officer immediately rushed into the shop. At that time, the thief caught sight of the police officer arriving and realized that the situation had been lost. He ran out and fired a shot at the police officer to resist arrest. However, the thief was actually an amateur and did not know the method of firing a gun. Therefore, although he used his finger to move the firing pin, the bullet was not loaded into the barrel, so the bullet could not be fired. Seeing the opportunity, the police officer jumped forward and hugged the thief, snatching the pistol and finally capturing him alive. At that time, the second district of the first district also received a police report. The director, Liu Yunfang, led a large number of long-term police officers to rush to the scene of the incident and rounded up the area. However, because it was too late, the three thieves were nowhere to be seen, so they gained nothing. They took the captured thief back to the station. After a strict interrogation, he confessed that his name was Huang Defa, 33 years old, from Dongyang. He was previously a tailor and is now unemployed. The rest of his words were vague. It was later learned that the pistol held by the thief was a six-inch Brownring pistol with six bullets inside, but the gun handle was engraved with the number 125939 of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. The subordinates were ordered to temporarily detain the thief, and he personally led the long-term police officers to pursue and arrest the remaining thieves, and secretly investigate the origin of the gun. It is reported that many thieves have been arrested and are currently being interrogated.

Landing, the wheel company gave Dr. Te special treatment, and the fares, etc., were given special discounts.

Captains Can Be Exempted From Examination by the Ministry for Certificate Renewal: Within this year's January, a new chapter was specially issued stating that when applying for renewal after the expiration of the captain's certificate, an examination by the Examination Committee of the Ministry of Communications should also be taken in accordance with the Regulations on Crew Qualification, and if qualified, a certificate will be issued, etc. The Shanghai Masters Association raised an objection to this matter, and submitted a request to the Ministry to abolish the captain's certificate examination item. The Ministry has replied to Shanghai, approving the preservation of this case in the Ministry, so captains can be exempted from examination when renewing their certificates.

The Best-Selling Chinese Diplomatic Yearbook 168

The "Chinese Diplomatic Yearbook," edited by the Chinese Diplomatic Yearbook Society and distributed by the Shenghuo Bookstore on Avenue Joffre in Shanghai, has been published. The book is rich in material, thoroughly researched, and contains concise descriptions of the history of Chinese diplomacy, from the Qing Dynasty to the Republic of China. Regarding diplomatic issues in the past 22 years, there are detailed and accurate accounts. The book has spared no effort in collecting the organizational regulations and treaties of diplomatic administration. The entire book is divided into two major parts: the main text and the appendix, with a total of more than 600,000 words. Text and tables are given equal importance, the layout is novel, and the printing is excellent. The collection of photos of important figures in the diplomatic world is particularly complete. Therefore, since its publication, political organs, embassies, consulates, and school libraries have purchased copies, showing its popularity. The deluxe edition of the book, bound in fine Daolin paper, is priced at $2.50 per copy, and the regular edition is $1.50. Bookstores in major cities have sales.

Shrimp Sauce Splashed on Dancing Girl's Dress 170

A Major Dispute Arises in the Ballroom

Yang Xianmei, a woman from Liyang living at No. 10 Hepingli, Avenue Edward VII, in the Public Concession, is a graceful and beautiful 25-year-old dancing girl. At 3:30 AM on the 9th of this month, while Yang was sitting for a short break after dancing in the ballroom, Pan Meiying, a fellow dancer, sat next to Yang and was eating a large dish. Yang immediately questioned Pan, asking why she wasn't more careful. Pan stubbornly refused to admit fault, and a quarrel ensued. Pan's companion, Chen Aying, was nearby, cheering her on. Yang, with her two fists, was ultimately no match for Pan and Chen's four hands. Counterfeiting of Lei Yunshang Medicines; Police Uncover Counterfeiting Operation 171

The Lei Yunshang Pharmacy at No. 252 Xinbeimenwai, Route de Sieyes, in the French Concession specializes in selling various pills, powders, plasters, and elixirs, especially its Liushen Pills, which are famous at home and abroad and sell in Japan for about a million dollars a year. This has led to unscrupulous people coveting the profits, often making counterfeit medicines to imitate and profit from. The store has offered a large reward for investigation and arrest, and there have been arrests and legal actions from time to time. However, unscrupulous elements still dare to defy the law and privately produce counterfeit medicines. Recently, Zhang Yaonan (41 years old), Li Jinyuan (25 years old), Song Tingshu (31 years old), and others from Nanjing were counterfeiting Liushen Pills, Wolong Pills, and other medicines, selling them under false pretenses in the market. The owner of Lei Yunshang Pharmacy, Lei Xianzhi, discovered this and reported it to the French police, requesting an investigation. The detective Lu Changsheng from the French police's detective department discovered that Zhang and others' counterfeiting operation was located at No. 30 Yuyangli, Rue du Maréchal Joffre. On the afternoon of the 10th, he secretly went to the address and arrested Zhang, Li, and Song. He confiscated three packages of pills, 2,500 ox horn boxes, 2,000 paper boxes, 21 bundles of imitations of labels of various sizes, a package of invoices, a half-foreign-style iron box of Wolong Pills, and many tools for manufacturing medicines. All were taken to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, explained the case, stating that the police had not yet investigated the case and requested a postponement pending a detailed investigation of the case, requesting a trial. He also presented the confiscated evidence. The detective also reported the arrest of the defendants and the details of the search. Judge Wu Fanglian reviewed the report and questioned the defendants briefly. He then approved a postponement of 14 days for further investigation and questioning. The defendants were remanded in custody.

Flour Mills Losing 100,000 Dollars Daily; Market Shrinks, Flour Prices Decline Steadily; Mills to Shut Down in Months 174

China's flour milling industry has the most factories in Wuxi, Shanghai, Zhengzhou, Bengbu, Nanjing, and other places, with a total of more than 20 factories, capable of producing 300,000 bags of flour per day. Previously, they were sold to the Yingkou and Andong markets, but since the September 18th Incident, they have been seized by Japanese goods. When domestic goods arrive there, they must pay import taxes, making it difficult to compete. Although the government authorities have indicated that if domestically produced flour is sold in the eastern provinces, the taxes paid can be appropriately refunded, it has not yet been implemented. Flour prices have been steadily declining recently, with each bag losing 35 cents. All flour mills across the country can produce 300,000 bags of flour per day, which, at market prices, leads to a daily loss of more than 100,000 dollars. Therefore, in a few months, all flour mills across the country will go bankrupt, workers will lose their jobs, and the safety and security of society will be at stake, which is a cause for concern. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce believes that the national flour milling industry is related to the livelihood of hundreds of thousands of workers and will face extinction, so it has specially dispatched commissioners to investigate the history of flour mills in various places in order to provide relief.

Umbrella Industry Dispute Resolved; Workers Resumed Work Yesterday Morning; Result of the Jingjiang Fellow-Countrymen Association's Mediation; Labor and Management Sign Four Conditions 176

The strike of umbrella industry workers in this city was resolved yesterday through the mediation of the Jingjiang Fellow-Countrymen Association, with both sides agreeing to conditions and officially resuming work. Each factory will host the press at 6 PM tomorrow. The details are as follows:

Mediation Resolved

Since the umbrella workers' demands for management to sign a treaty were not met, the strike has been repeatedly mediated by party and government organs without success. The Jingjiang Fellow-Countrymen Association specially dispatched Zhang Yan, Chen Zhisun, Qu Shiji, and others, as well as the umbrella inventor Chen Lianfang, as fellow-countrymen and friends (because most of the labor and management in this industry are from Jingjiang, and most of the workers are Chen Lianfang's past employees) to mediate with both sides. Chen Lianfang even knelt down to the workers, forcing them to agree. It was not resolved until 6 AM yesterday.

Conditions Signed

Labor and management signed four conditions: (1) Workers whose monthly wages were originally above $10 will receive a 40% increase; those below $10 will receive a 50% increase. (2) Female workers will receive at least 1.2 cents for each umbrella they sew, excluding the frame (those who already have better terms will remain unchanged). (3) Workers who were originally paid by the piece will continue to be paid by the piece; those who are paid monthly will be handled according to the first condition. (4) Wages for the strike period will be paid at half rate.

Full Resumption of Work

After labor and management signed the conditions, all 1,000+ umbrella workers from 53 companies, including Fengli, Yingfeng, Minhua 1st, 2nd, 3rd, Minhua, Songlixin, etc., were notified separately by the mediators and labor-management representatives. They all resumed work at 7 AM yesterday. Unemployed workers no longer gathered to cause trouble. Both labor and management will submit the details of the agreement and the signed conditions to the City Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau for record.

Press Conference

The umbrella industry association, including Fengli and Minhua, believes that the news media's attitude towards this labor-management dispute was fair, so they have specifically scheduled to host reporters from various newspapers and news agencies at the Zhimeilou Restaurant on Daxin Street, Fuzhou Road, at 6 PM tomorrow to announce the details of the dispute and express their gratitude. Invitation cards will be distributed today.

Central Bank Inspection Report 179

The Central Bank's 193rd Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states:

Based on Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. The 193rd inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on April 14th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934). The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of silver yuan convertible banknotes issued is 68,080,063 silver yuan, including 61,666,131 silver yuan in silver yuan notes and 6,413,932 silver yuan in subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of convertible banknote reserves is 68,080,063 silver yuan, including 55,164,063 silver yuan in cash reserves. This cash reserve is kept at the Issuance Department of this bank, amounting to 51,518,061 silver yuan; at branch banks in various ports, amounting to 1,883,089 silver yuan; and deposited with other banks, amounting to 1,762,913 silver yuan. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 12,916,000 silver yuan. (B) The total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknotes issued is 373,324.7 customs gold units. The total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknote reserves is 373,324.7 customs gold units. The reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, valued at 0.50779 gold units, totaling 373,324.7 customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's regulations on convertible banknotes, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guaranteed reserve 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, while the guaranteed reserve is less than 40%, which is inconsistent with the regulations. This report is hereby made. April 11th, 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934). Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun; Supervisors Xie Mingdong, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

Letters to the Editor 196

Dear Editor,

I recently read the "Local News" column in your newspaper, which contained a list of Chinese visitors attending the Nagasaki International Industrial Exposition, and my name was on the list.

After reading it, I was horrified. The reason is that I did not know the details of the expo before and thought it was a purely international industrial exposition of a sightseeing nature, so I once joined. After reading the newspaper, I learned that the expo had a different purpose, so I withdrew immediately to avoid being used. Now I am still in Shanghai and have not participated in going to Japan. I have nothing to do with all the subsequent actions of the group. I am afraid that there may be a misunderstanding, so I am writing to clarify this matter. Please correct it.

Sincerely,

Hong Yisheng, April 10th.

Dear Editor,

We are writing on behalf of the parties involved, Xu Li-shi and Xu Cao-shi, who claim that the news item published in the Shen Bao on November 11th regarding the abandonment of a sick person in a vegetable garden who subsequently died is completely inconsistent with the facts. It has been verified that Liu Wen-kui's wife, Cai-shi, was ill, and Liu Wen-kui, together with his parents, carried Cai-shi to an open space on the east side of the residence when Cai-shi was dying. Although the parties are the landlords, they were never involved in the matter. Later, some unscrupulous people incited Liu Wen-kui to threaten the parties to borrow money without success, so they fabricated rumors in an attempt to slander them. If Liu Wen-kui has fabricated false accusations, the parties will file a lawsuit for false accusation. The report in the newspaper is based on hearsay and is inaccurate. Please ask your lawyer to send a letter to the newspaper requesting a correction, etc. We hereby inform you of the situation and hope that your newspaper will investigate and make a correction.

Sincerely,

Lawyer Qian Baohe, April 11th.

Reading Q&A

Another Example of Studying International Issues ㈡ 197

Analyzing international politics not only requires considering the basic conflicts between nations at a certain stage, not only requires considering the ebb and flow of contradictions in a certain country, but most importantly, it is also impossible to forget all the changes within countries with different systems other than capitalism. For example, if we want to understand the increasingly urgent significance of the imperialist anti-Soviet war, we should not only understand it from the abstract proposition that capitalism and socialism are irreconcilable, but we must specifically understand it from the great victory of Soviet economic construction, the democracy of the masses expressed in the new political system, and the rapid increase in the material living standards of the masses. We should also examine the impact of the leap forward in new culture on the capitalist system. Only then can we understand that the imperialists are anti-Soviet not because they are anti-abstract socialism, but because they are anti-socialist countries that have been practicing and have won victory. The existence and growth of this monster is an invisible threat to capitalism. This is not only a major point that cannot be ignored in analyzing today's international situation, but even when analyzing the politics of a country on a small scale, one cannot let go of the influence exerted by this aspect. For example, the relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union is extremely tense, but Japan still does not dare to try it lightly. If we want to understand this relationship, on the one hand, we can say that the tension in the relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union is due to the success of Soviet economic construction, but at the same time, we must also know that the reason why Japan does not dare to try it lightly is precisely due to the success of Soviet economic construction. It seems contradictory, but it is actually very natural.

Are international issues that simple? No! Absolutely not! The above is just a brief examination from various aspects. If an observer only pays attention to one aspect and ignores other aspects, he will naturally only become a formalist, only seeing the trees and not seeing the forest. If an observer only grasps the main framework of international relations at a certain stage and ignores the specific facts of development, he will certainly see all the problems as empty and unable to grasp their particularity. The conclusions he makes will only be some abstract principles, becoming formalism. By reciting formulas, it will lose its temporality. As long as the general situation has not changed, it can be applied at almost any time. Although this type of observer is more advanced than the former, in reality, he is still of no use at all. At most, he is just a mechanist, mechanizing all dynamic situations. A scientific observer should not only accurately grasp the various aspects mentioned above, but also synthesize the situation of each historical stage from the various aspects or processes, in a lively and dynamic manner, point out the particularity of each historical stage, and point out the nature of every event that occurs in each historical stage. Because the occurrence of every problem in the international community today is not due to a simple factor, but is woven into a network with countless intersecting warp and weft threads. A scientific observer should not just say some empty words of principle and consider it done. He should specifically analyze the occurrence of facts, reveal their truth, and point out the direction of development.

Now it's time to go back to the question raised by Mr. Zhao. Mr. Zhao said, "The international situation is changing rapidly," which is absolutely true. Then Mr. Zhao said, "It is really elusive," which is not very correct. Although international issues are very complex and change quickly, in fact, as long as you observe carefully, they are still "graspable." Mr. Zhao's understanding of the "Japanese-American compromise" is also completely wearing formal theoretical glasses, so he cannot point out the shortcomings of many commentators' opinions, but only sees them as contradictions, which is meaningfully "deceiving" him.

We cannot deny the truth of "Japan and the United States cannot share interests in the Far East" and "A war must break out in the Pacific." At the same time, we also agree that "the economic relationship between Britain and the United States is even more serious than that between Japan and the United States." However, these words are only the main principles in studying the relationship between Japan and the United States and between Britain and the United States. The understanding of the current event of the Japanese-American compromise should not be understood without leaving these main principles, but we should not just recite these words of principle and consider it an answer to this question. This is largely why Mr. Zhao is dissatisfied with current events. Now let's give Mr. Zhao a hint of a research path on the "Japanese-American compromise."

Since the Japanese-American compromise is not as simple as Mr. Zhao said in his letter, then how should the foundation of its actual occurrence be understood? First, we must examine it from three aspects: Britain and the United States, Britain and Japan, and Japan and the United States. The relationship between Britain and the United States contains: "the contradiction of comprehensive economic opposition"; however, recent international events have not intensified their transition to a new battleground. The relationship between Britain and Japan has recently revealed a naked diplomatic war from trade competition, and they have reached a stage where they do not give way to each other. Although the relationship between Japan and the United States is indeed irreconcilable in the Pacific, the surface of the two countries' economic structure does not have much conflict. In terms of trade between the two countries, they are still very good, and they have been old customers for many years. Their discord is produced in the contradictions of capitalism itself and the future development of the two countries, so if there are changes in other aspects, a temporary compromise between Japan and the United States is possible. The recent international relations are naturally set against the backdrop of the world economic panic. The panic has made Britain and the United States feel hostile to each other everywhere; the panic has made Britain and Japan abandon the old alliance and turn to glaring at each other and refusing to give way; the panic has intensified the opposition between Japan and the United States in the Pacific; but at the same time, it has also prompted Japan to abandon Britain and turn to the United States to concede conditions. The United States has also failed to revive its country, the world situation is becoming increasingly difficult, and preparations for war have not yet been fully grasped. In the process of war organization,

American businessmen cannot help but think in their hearts, "We have no unpleasantness with Japan in business! Since they are negotiating with us, why don't we perfunctorily deal with them once? Haha, this is also breaking up the old friendship between Britain and Japan, which is a kind of threat to Britain!" (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Drifting Record of Imperial Incense 198

— Qin Shouou

Although the imperial decree for the Holy Carriage to travel east had been decided, there were many things that needed to be prepared before departure. The first step was to have the Empress Dowager issue a formal edict, specifying on what date her special train would depart from Beijing and return to Fengtian. At the same time, a new law had to be added, which was that when the Empress Dowager's special train was running on the road, no other vehicles were allowed to move on any section of the road, and violators would be punished with extreme penalty. Of course, this time, the officials on the Beijing-Fengtian Railway could not avoid being assigned as basic service personnel. In addition, the Empress Dowager had to randomly pick out several important court officials to travel with her. As for all other preparatory work, it was handled by me and General Qing Shan, and I don't have time to write about it in detail here.

As soon as the preparatory work began, the railway workers were busy first. Because according to our estimate, to load all the officials, eunuchs, palace maids, and various utensils, materials, etc., this special imperial train had to be equipped with sixteen carriages. At the same time, because these vehicles had never been driven after being purchased, for the sake of prudence, it was necessary to conduct a thorough inspection first; this part of the work was actually completed very quickly. The next thing was to completely repaint the sixteen cars in yellow, which represented the royal family. The only thing that could maintain its original appearance was the locomotive. I think if the Empress Dowager thought of this, she would never allow the locomotive to not change its color.

What a pity! We couldn't have a yellow locomotive, dragging us, dashing back and forth in the wilderness of China. I still feel regretful to this day!

Although the Empress Dowager was determined to leave Beijing, she still had to teach the ministers in the court to express some opinions on this matter as usual. Whenever something more important happened, she always had to ask them for their opinions. (9)

New Life Movement 199

— Xun Zi

The New Life Movement, since its vigorous promotion by various parties, has recently reached a fever pitch.

The so-called New Life is about restoring China's inherent ancient virtues: propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame; and making life orderly, clean, and simple. When a rickshaw puller had his registration card taken away by an Indian policeman, he knelt down in the middle of the road, kowtowing to the Indian policeman like pounding garlic, repeatedly calling him "Officer." When we saw this, we didn't feel that the rickshaw puller was flattering foreigners or shameless; but felt he was oppressed by life and pitiable!

Looking at the many Jiangbei shanties on the vacant land in Zhabei, one usually has to bend over to enter. When it rains or snows, people are practically crouching in the mud. This kind of life undoubtedly lacks the conditions for order and cleanliness. However, to remove this stain on Shanghai's face, it is necessary to plan well for the people in the shanties afterwards. It cannot be solved by setting a fire and burning everything to the ground.

Therefore, the foundation of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame is built on "sufficient clothing and food." Without clothing or food, how can one practice propriety, uphold righteousness, cultivate integrity, or understand shame? If you complain that their clothes are not neat and their diet is not clean, they will simply answer you with one sentence: "No money!" The ancients spoke of "frugality within propriety." For people living below the poverty line, poverty is real, and there is no room for frugality.

It is hoped that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and other gentlemen who advocate the New Life Movement will focus on the people's livelihood, and then improving life will not be a problem!

A Short Note on Listening to Music 200

— Yang Yusheng

The meeting was over, and the noise was very loud. I followed the crowd out of the concert at the National "Music Academy," my ears still ringing. It seemed that the lingering sound of "La Traviata Drinking Song" still remained.

It was late, the wind was strong, and it was raining. The streetlights were a dispirited pale green, and several immature pine trees in the distance looked like someone was squatting and shivering. La Traviata wouldn't appear at this time, would she! I thought to myself.

I ran back to the dormitory in the rain, took off my clothes and went to sleep. But the sound in my ears was always restless and noisy, and I couldn't fall asleep no matter what.

Oh no! Could it be that La Traviata actually found me! Listen! What is that sound! Damn! How did she get here to "warm up her voice" again!

This is an old, clear day with an Eastern feel, let's enjoy ourselves while we can! Ah! If we have to have this beautiful scenery to enjoy ourselves, then we are utterly foolish and pitiful! Let's not mention what filial piety is, as long as everyone is comfortable and happy, and we don't care if the weather is good or not, as long as we are looking at the wine glass with smiling eyes, and the smiling eyes in the glass look at each other. Heaven makes wine and makes love, for the sake of Heaven and Earth Mother always loving each other. People say we are too muddleheaded in our dealings with the world, forget it! What's wrong with being muddleheaded? You can say what you want, and we'll do what we want. Even if you are the most powerful prosecutor, please come and look at our wine glasses! Ah! I guarantee that your heart will immediately turn around, and you will be filled with joy.

Some people say I'm "seeing ghosts" and pretending to be confused. Forget it! What's wrong with being muddleheaded?

But then again, Mr. Liu Bannong's translation is truly a perfect portrayal of the character of the "modern" Chinese! Mr. Liu is truly a "foresighted" "Chinese"!

— Zhang Henshui

Unexpectedly, the leg of the stool tripped over his thigh, and he almost fell flat on his face. If he hadn't known a few tricks and quickly supported himself against the wall, he probably would have had a bad fall. As he spoke, he walked back to his room, took three eggs, and went to the kitchen. Gui Zhi was really uneasy when she saw this. But she had already lied, so she couldn't say that her eyes weren't hurting. She just smiled and said, "Old sir, please rest, I would feel terribly guilty. How could I ask you to bother yourself?" Zhao Weng wouldn't listen and waited for Xiao Lin to boil the eggs and bring them over before eating. Gui Zhi ate the eggs, thinking, "The old sir is sincere, but I am being insincere. Strictly speaking, I'm letting him down." Therefore, after eating, she didn't dare to pretend to be sick and came with Xiao Lin to clear the dishes. Zhao Weng repeatedly waved his hand and said, "Why are you doing this? Being diligent doesn't depend on one or two days. You go and lie down. I have something to do and need to go out." Gui Zhi said it was alright and listened to Zhao Weng leaving on his own. Not long after, Zhao Weng came back with a paper package. Seeing Gui Zhi sitting in the hall, he stretched out the paper package from afar and smiled at her, "This is Hangzhou chrysanthemum. Take it and brew a pot of water to drink. If your eyes are inflamed, drinking a pot will help." Gui Zhi smiled and said, "I'm putting you to so much trouble." Zhao Weng didn't answer, and stretched his hand into his coat, fumbling for a long time, and took out a small porcelain bottle, pinched it with two fingers, and put it into Gui Zhi's hand, and said with a smile, "This is Dingzhou eye drops, it will help if you apply it, just take it and use it." Gui Zhi didn't expect her father-in-law to leave in a hurry after eating, only to buy medicine for her. This old man treats people with kindness, benevolence, and loyalty, without any other intentions, how could one not be grateful? At that time, she repeatedly thanked him and took the eye drops and chrysanthemum to the room. (360)

Circular Nouns 203

— Qifenglou Master

The meaning of Chinese characters is profound. If you try to read two characters repeatedly, the explanation of the meaning of the characters will be very different. Now I will list a few examples for fun.

(Zhejiang) The name of a province. (Jiangzhe) An abbreviation for the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang.

(Qingren) Means lover. (Renqing) Refers to human relationships. (Banfa) Means a way to do things. (Faban) Means to punish according to law. (Guanke) Means visitor. (Keguan) The object of the subjective.

(Honghua) The name of a medicine. (Huahong) The name of a fruit, also refers to the bonus given to employees by merchants.

(Wenming) The opposite of barbarism. (Mingwen) Refers to bright and clear writing.

(Qianren) A debtor in law. (Renqian) A creditor in law.

(Mujiu) Means maternal uncle. (Jiumu) Means maternal aunt, female. (Ernu) Means sons and daughters. (Nver) Refers to a girl.

Women's Hair 204

— Ying

Women's clothing is constantly changing, of course. Not to mention clothing, even hair is constantly changing. Since last autumn, the most fashionable women in the world have returned to their natural brown color without adding any modifications. Indeed, the news from Paris has already eliminated platinum blonde. In general, people acknowledge that this color has been popular for too long. In the United States, where platinum hair bleaching is prevalent, people have first felt that it is no longer fashionable. The average woman in New York, since April, has even been making the entire American female population aim to express golden hair as a standard. At the same time, Broadway has raised the slogan "Let your hair grow naturally and hang down."

In London, if we make a comparison, the top-notch hairdressers in the West say this to people: "Women come to get their hair done, and they usually do what they like. But now they all say they no longer like short hair, because they want to grow it out and let it hang down behind their necks so that they can curl it up. This kind of curl is very light, otherwise they will find it too heavy. But because the only way to curl the hair up is to grow out the short hair! Therefore, short hair is going to be unfashionable in London now."

Now, very few women want to bleach their hair platinum blonde like before. Even if they like to bleach their hair like this, they don't like to use other colors either. Otherwise, they will have to spend a lot of time in the barber shop. Women want to grow their hair long, even very long, and they don't have to cut it, because they often wear hats when they go out, and the longer the hair, the bigger the hat can be.

Random Thoughts

The Fun of Flying Kites 205

— Huang Yingdai

The Benefits of Flying Kites

When spring comes, the most fashionable pastime is of course flying kites. Not to mention adults, even children know how to fly them, and they don't involve gambling, so they are more noble than other pastimes. Children who fly kites run and jump in the wild, which can increase their vitality and invigorate their spirits. In addition, the air in the wild is fresh and the scenery is beautiful, which can make children feel happy. Moreover, as long as you have hemp string and a kite, you can fly it once, twice, or countless times without spending any more money. It is the most economical pastime, no wonder the government officials are promoting kite flying this time!

How to Make Kites

The raw materials for making kites are only colored paper, bamboo, paste, and string. In Shanghai, the stores that sell kites are very expensive. In fact, you can just make them yourself. Use bamboo to make the frame, and paste on colored paper, and you're done. Simple hexagonal, octagonal, and nine-string kites can be made by anyone. More complex butterflies and centipedes can also be made by skilled people. It doesn't cost much money, but it must be made accurately, otherwise it won't fly high. If the kite is made with the same size top and bottom, then you need to use a tail. The bigger the wind, the more tails you need, but if it's bigger, you don't need a tail.

How to Attach Kite Lanterns

Flying kites also has various other fun things to do. First of all, kite lanterns. In the evening, you can attach kite lanterns. Colorful paper lanterns should be covered with lead sheet to prevent the wind from blowing them out. A small brick is tied below to prevent the wind from swinging them. This way, they can be attached to the kite string, and the distance must be uniform so that it looks neat from below. The number of lanterns depends on the size of the kite. If you attach too many, the kite will be unable to handle it and will fall. In Shanghai, some people use electric wires to attach red and green electric lights, but the weight must also be considered!

Bow-shaped Kite Harp

The kite harp is made of a bamboo strip, a piece of bamboo, or a silk ribbon. The bamboo strip is bent like a bow, and the bamboo strip or silk ribbon is used as the bowstring. Some are attached to the kite, and some are attached to the string, but the angle must be aligned with the wind direction, otherwise it will not sound. The kite harp, attached to the kite, fluctuates with the wind and emits undulating琴 sounds, rising and falling in the air, which you can hear from far away.

Gunpowder Made Sand

Use a strip of cotton paper to make a tube, put gunpowder and charcoal dust, ground finely, inside, tie one end tightly and tie it to the kite string, tie a fuse to the other end, light the fire and let the kite string out, and when the fuse lights the gunpowder and charcoal dust, the sky will scatter a sky of sparks, like a reversed firework tube. In the evening, it is a very interesting pastime, but if there are grass huts below, you must be careful, for fear of causing a fire, so this kind of pastime can only be tried in the open fields of the wilderness.

Other Varieties

I have already mentioned several kinds of kite pastimes in Shanghai, but in addition, there are several kinds such as flying疊鷂 [kites on kites], using red and green paper to make windmills, attaching them to the kite string, tying a string of firecrackers, lighting them, tying them to the string, and releasing them into the sky, crackling and popping... they are all very interesting pastimes!

Whether Japan Participates or Not, the Far East Games Will Be Held as Scheduled; Non-Athletic Association Secretary Issues Statement 206

(National News Agency, San Fernando, 10th) According to Li Jin Yan Nan, Secretary and Treasurer of the Philippine Amateur Athletic Association, today, the Far Eastern Games have been decided to be held here next month, regardless of whether Japan participates or not, this purpose will not change. The association was very indignant after hearing that Japan intended to withdraw from the competition because the puppet state's participation was rejected. The Philippine side has already spent a lot of money preparing for the conference, so the conference will proceed as usual, whether Japanese athletes participate or not. According to news obtained here from Japan, it seems that the Japanese sports authorities believe that the Philippine side is obstructing the participation of the puppet Manchukuo. According to Li, the Philippine Athletic Association did not interfere in the above matter. Furthermore, Shi, Chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce, told reporters that those involved in the Far Eastern Games have no need to fear. Even if the Japanese side refuses to participate, the association's income will certainly not be affected in any way, because the Chinese Chamber of Commerce believes that the Chinese side will fully support it.

(Dentsu, Tokyo, 11th) The Sports Association's plenary meeting to discuss countermeasures for the Shanghai round-table conference was held yesterday at Misaka Koraku, attended by Vice President Hiraji, Chief Officer Takashima, and others, centering on Dr. Yamamoto's instructions, discussed everything, and considered the issue to be of great importance, unable to decide lightly.

Postponed for one day, member groups will gather opinions tonight at the Marunouchi Central Pavilion for a board meeting. Depending on the shape of the board meeting, Japan may not participate in the Taisho 6 Imperial Cup Far East Games due to the untrustworthy behavior of China and the Philippines.

(Japan Federation News, Tokyo, 11th) The Japan Sports Association received a report from Dr. Yamamoto in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 10th on the progress of the round-table conference. Association authorities decided to hold a plenary meeting tonight after receiving Yamamoto's second report to decide on Japan's final attitude on whether to participate in the Far East Games or not. According to general observation, things have come to this point, Japan's non-participation (not withdrawal) in the Far East Games cannot be avoided.

Yamamoto's Second Report (Japan Federation News, Tokyo, 11th) The second report from Representative Yamamoto, which the Sports Association was waiting for, was received on the morning of the 11th. The Sports Association released the content of its report at 2 pm, as follows:

Although the Philippine side has not signed a contract on the articles, it has already approved its membership at this meeting, and has suddenly taken a position of abstention on the issue of participation in the competition. It is impossible to find any sincerity in this situation. Japan no longer needs to have any sentimental feelings about the Far East Games, but it seems cowardly to disengage from the difficulties. In my opinion, it is appropriate not to participate.

Japan Sports Association Attitude (Japan Federation News, Tokyo, 11th) The Japan Sports Association suddenly adopted a strong attitude towards the issue of participating in the Far East Games. Because Dr. Yamamoto's reply also advocated that it would be appropriate not to participate, the attitude of the Sports Association has become increasingly hardened. It is said that participation in this Far East Games was originally for the sake of seeking international trust with the Philippines, and Japan has no benefit to speak of. Now that the Filipinos have adopted such an unreasonable attitude, Japan should have no need to participate. If the Filipinos change their attitude of reflection because the Japanese side does not participate, and approve the participation of the puppet organization, then it should be discussed separately. However, whether the original proposal not to participate will be cancelled at that time is still Japan's freedom. This kind of opinion seems very powerful. The general tone of the board meeting convened at 6 pm on the 11th was quite strong, so the resolution not to participate in the Far East Games should be considered final.

Japan Sports Association Questions the Philippine Islands (Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, Express Telegram, 11th) The Japan Sports Association's emergency board meeting to decide on Japan's attitude towards the Far East Games was held at Fan Nei House at 7 pm today. International Volleyball Tournament Ends; China Champions; USA Loses All Three Sets; Awards Given and Dismissed 209

The first Shanghai International Volleyball Tournament held by the West YMCA ended last night. As a result of the final between China and the United States, China won two consecutive sets, and the championship has been obtained. Chinese athletes were sharpening their fists and preparing for the third set, but the American team cheered and dispersed, admitting defeat. According to the rules, China won the set 15-0. There were more than 100 spectators. The results are as follows:

Fifteen to Eleven

China 45 Fifteen to Ten United States 21

Fifteen to Zero

Losing First, Winning Later Although the American team was fierce, it had no way out under the Chinese players' thunderous kill shots. Chinese players' average personal skills, whether killing or saving the ball, are superb, making the audience marvel. However, they sometimes reveal panic and often lose points due to carelessness. They initially lost four points, and the formation was very disorganized. Afterwards, they tried their best to cheer up, tied it at six to six, and seven to seven, and then turned defeat into victory, reaching ten to seven. When China took the lead at fourteen to eleven, the stalemate was intense, and it was difficult for each to score. However, China finally won 15-11.

All the Way Smooth The second set rotated serves, and neither side made much progress for a long time. However, the American team's formation revealed flaws, unable to withstand the Chinese team's fierce attacks. Before long, the Chinese team won 6-1. Although the American team managed to regain the right to serve several times, it had no chance to score. The Chinese team advanced steadily, taking the lead at 13-1, thinking it would be easy to finish it in one go. Unexpectedly, they lost the wind due to carelessness, and the American team soared up, 13-7, 14-9, before finally winning 15-10 and winning the championship. The United States forfeited the third set.

Team Scores In this competition, scores are not counted, but sets are counted. The Chinese team only lost one set to the United States. The United States failed to maintain the lead in the kill. The United States lost one set to both the Russian expatriates and the Jewish team, and lost three sets to the Chinese team. In terms of strength, the United States is no match for China. Chinese Athletic Federation Basketball Tournament to be Held at Various Schools 211

The annual basketball league organized by the Shanghai Secondary School Athletic Federation was originally approved to be held at the Chinese Basketball Hall. Unexpectedly, the Basketball Hall was destroyed by fire, preventing the original plan from being realized. Yesterday, the

Federation's Basketball Committee members Jiang Jingnan, Wu Shijie, and Liu Wenxiao (Lu Xiangqiandai) held a meeting at the Coordination Association to discuss remedial measures. It was decided that all matches could only be held at various schools. In addition to the original competition regulations, the following items have been added, and the competition schedule has been shortened. They are recorded below:

(1) Time: The competition will begin on the 18th of this month and end on the 22nd. The dates for the finals for the Chinese and Physical Education groups will be determined separately by the committee. Each match will start at 4:00 PM.

(2) Location: The competition venue will be changed to various schools. If it is held at School A this year, it will be held at School B next time. The finals venue will be changed to a public location.

(3) Referees: The home team is responsible for hiring referees. The home team is responsible for the transportation costs. It is hoped that all schools will prepare early to avoid delays.

(4) Postponement: If the competition cannot be held at the scheduled time and venue due to rain, wet ground, or special circumstances, it must be completed between the 23rd and 29th of this month. However, postponement due to any reason requires the consent of the other party. Postponement due to wet ground must be notified to the opposing team in the morning. If both parties can negotiate to borrow an indoor basketball hall, that is also acceptable.

(5) Reports: The home team is responsible for submitting a written report of the results of the match to Basketball Chairman Jiang Jingnan (Guanghua University, Da Xi Road) on the same evening for reference. The list of players and score sheets from both teams must be copied and included in the report.

Zhenjiang Dianlei School's Letter Published 216

Dear Editor,

Regarding the Zhenjiang communication in your newspaper's sports column on the 27th of this month, which stated that students from our school's military academy beat a referee during a basketball game, upon reading it, we were extremely surprised. On that day (the 17th), when the Leiming team, composed of military academy students from our school's training team, was playing against the Xiaoniao team, the referee, Zhou Mingzhang, misunderstood the rules and made an unfair judgement. The team's players asked for an explanation and temporarily stopped the game. At that time, Mr. Yuan Zhongkang, director of the guidance department of the Provincial Sports Ground, acknowledged that Mr. Zhou did not understand the rules and made an unfair judgement. He was willing to apologize to our school's basketball team in writing or in the newspaper on behalf of the Provincial Sports Ground and his personal reputation. Our platoon leader, Huang, believed that the matter was minor, and since the director knew that Mr. Zhou's judgment was unfair, our school could give him due understanding in order to preserve Mr. Zhou's reputation and bring the matter to a close. At that time, our team only sent two representatives to ask Mr. Zhou for an explanation, and did not enter the room. The facts are all there and can be easily distinguished. How could it be said that the door was broken down and they rushed into the room? Furthermore, our school does not have a Wang instructor. Although platoon leader Huang was present

, the mistake was not on our side, and there was no apology. How could it be said that an oral apology was made through Instructor Wang? To investigate the referee, if the referee's judgment is unfair, it is common for players to ask for an explanation. At that time, everyone was watching, and the facts were all there. How could one fabricate facts and make false statements afterwards? The above situation is only a general summary. The details at that time cannot be described one by one. Because what your newspaper published does not match the facts, we are afraid of causing confusion. We hereby request that you investigate and correct it in your newspaper immediately. Sincerely, Dianlei School Training Team, attached by Xu Shidan, March 29th.

Education News

Other Locations 217

Key Points for Improving Education in the Capital City 218

Report by the Ministry of Education Inspector

The Ministry of Education previously sent personnel to inspect education in Nanjing City. The results of the inspection have been reported to the Ministry of Education. The following are the opinions on improving education in the capital city, which we have learned of:

(1) It has been found that the city is able to expand compulsory primary schools, but the equipment in each school is mostly simple, and the teaching methods are also mostly rigid. Both should be improved. The bureau should designate compulsory primary schools with better management to compile reports on the management process, graduate performance, and all difficult problems within a reasonable period of time, and report them to the ministry for inspection. Alternatively, well-equipped and well-managed primary schools should be designated to pilot compulsory primary schools and two-part full-day systems to observe their performance and

consider how to promote them. At the same time, efforts should be made to expand primary schools so that all school-age children in the city have the opportunity to attend school.

(2) The school buildings in the city are mostly simple and not very suitable, which affects educational facilities and children's safety. The bureau should earnestly plan methods to improve them.

(3) In recent years, many primary schools in the city have implemented corporal punishment to make up for the shortcomings of educational methods. However, the impact is ultimately negative. Each school should be clearly informed to avoid using corporal punishment and adopt other appropriate corrective methods to prevent abuses.

(4) The desks and chairs in the city's primary school classrooms are issued by the bureau, but the styles are often unsuitable and the materials are not strong. They often need to be repaired soon after being used, which is not economical. Methods should be found to improve them.

(5) The teaching equipment in public and private secondary schools, except for the biology and books in Anhui Middle School, the physics and chemistry in Zhongying Middle School and Zhongda Shixiao, the books in Jinling Girls' Middle School, the home affairs in Huiwen Girls' Middle School, and the drawing and labor in the Municipal No. 1 Middle School, is mostly simple. Teaching methods not only tend to focus on lectures and indoctrination in language and social science subjects, but also lack appropriate automatic and experimental work in natural science subjects. Teachers generally lack sufficient teaching and research spirit and should be addressed and improved separately.

(6) The number of students in each class in private secondary schools often reaches seventy or eighty, which is detrimental to teaching management, and the fees charged exceed the prescribed limits significantly. Strict restrictions should be imposed to improve educational efficiency and reduce the burden on students.

(7) Youth guidance is an urgent task of secondary school education. Apart from the Municipal No. 1 Middle School and Zhonghua Girls' Middle School, which have considerable facilities, most schools in the city have not paid attention to it. In addition, the responsibility for moral education in each school is still mostly borne by one or two moral education staff members, while teachers are ignored. The regulations on the integration of moral education and teaching in the secondary school curriculum promulgated by the Ministry of Education should be strictly implemented.

(8) The purpose of labor education is to acquire real skills and experience from practical activities and to cultivate the habit of diligence among young people. It should be carried out earnestly. Apart from Zhongda Shixiao, the Municipal No. 1 Middle School, and Huiwen Girls' Middle School, which pay attention to it, most schools in the city are perfunctory. They have neither venues nor tools, and use simple rattan work and wire work as their only work. Some do not even offer this subject, such as Zhongnan Middle School. Each school should be ordered to improve separately.

(9) There are a large number of private secondary schools in the city. The bureau should carefully assess a few schools with satisfactory performance starting from the 23rd academic year and provide appropriate

subsidies to encourage them.

(10) Private secondary schools have limited financial resources, and it is practically difficult for them to immediately convert to vocational schools. The bureau should consider the situation of each school and order them to pilot vocational courses, vocational supplementary classes, or convert to primary schools, and provide subsidies to excellent schools to encourage them.

(11) Private schools are able to make efforts to improve their facilities before applying for registration, but after approval, they often gradually become lax. Therefore, unregistered schools should be strictly banned, and registered schools should be subject to serious assessment and supervision at all times to meet the current standards.

(12) The focus of educational inspection is guidance. According to the school authorities in the city, "The Social Affairs Bureau inspectors inspect the school once per semester, but often do not express their opinions during the inspection and rarely provide reports on guidance and improvement." Attention should be paid to this in the future.

(13) The Nanjing Private Art College has not yet completed the registration procedures. The bureau has been ordered to instruct them to comply. It has been found that the school buildings are simple and very unsuitable, and the equipment and funds are insufficient. The bureau should order them to find ways to improve the content, raise funds, and rebuild the school buildings, and urge them to complete the registration procedures as soon as possible for verification and deprivation.

Zhou Houxu Talks About the Impressions of Studying Education in Japan (II) 219

(3) General military training is strictly enforced from middle school upwards. Military instructors are directly appointed by the Ministry of the Army, and students absolutely obey their instructors, fearing them like tigers. Instructors can arbitrarily whip students who do not perform well in military training. Each school has live-fire drills and live ammunition shooting,

field exercises, night exercises, etc. Students usually wear uniforms and hats. Boys are not allowed to keep their hair long and salute teachers. All aspects of life are like soldiers. Youths outside of school between the ages of sixteen and twenty-five are given strict military, vocational, and civic training at night by youth training centers. There are nearly 20,000 youth training centers across the country, mostly using primary and secondary school buildings. In addition, the organization of youth groups and juvenile groups also has military implications in times of national emergency. Japan pays such widespread attention to military training that in the event of an emergency, the entire country becomes soldiers. The Qing Dynasty Shrine seen in Tokyo, the Junior National Exhibition Hall seen in Baozuka, the National Defense Exhibition Hall, the Local History Exhibition Hall, etc., display various modern war tools, scientific weapons, comparisons of military power of various countries, the glorious history of Japan's foreign wars, and war trophies, as well as the great achievements of military men in defending the country. All of this encourages its citizens to study war, prepare for national defense, and participate in foreign aggression, which is truly shocking. Military training is now offered as a course in many schools in our country, but it is often perfunctory. Instructors cannot command, and students do not know how to obey. After many years, there have been few tangible results. The general public is numb and ignorant of the impending disaster. What is national defense? Our government should quickly establish military service and military training control measures, and the people should recognize their responsibilities, the danger of the situation, and quickly engage in military training and preparations for national defense.

(4) Cultivating diligent habits Japanese women have always been known for their diligence. In girls' schools, emphasis is placed on household chores. The equipment for students to practice sewing, cooking, washing, dyeing, gardening, home economics, hygiene, etc. is available from elementary school to university. The supervision of students is also very strict. In addition to regular classes, daily life, such as cooking, sweeping, and all school management chores, are done by students in rotation. The floors are spotless and the glass is crystal clear. The girls' schools we visited mostly do not use servants, and students handle everything themselves. In contrast, the manufacturing of dual-material young ladies in our country's girls' schools is truly incomparable. As for boys' schools, most of the sweeping and other chores are also done by students. Middle schools with more than a thousand students often only use five or six school workers, at most ten. Their training of young people in diligent habits is like this. Our country's habit of idleness is the biggest problem, and education has also mistakenly gone down the path of creating pampered youth. To cure this disease, we must make every effort to promote diligence in schools. This is what we should emulate from that country.

(5) Promoting production education In schools at all levels, the teaching materials for each subject,

all emphasize the country's resources, economic development, and knowledge and skills of agriculture and industry, in order to improve the methods of production. Vocational schools across the country teach production knowledge and skills. The five-year middle school engineering courses we visited were already able to manufacture extremely sophisticated machinery, electrical machinery, clocks, physical and chemical instruments, radio tubes, cosmetics, high-quality furniture, dyed and woven silk fabrics, Western-style sculptures, architecture, etc. Students in these schools can do anything that skilled craftsmen can make. Graduates of vocational schools at all levels are quite popular with society, and demand exceeds supply, especially those who operate their own factories and farms. In addition to vocational courses, universities and specialized schools also have vocational teacher training centers. For the general public to improve their living skills, supplementary night schools are attached to various vocational schools. Japanese vocational education aims to solve people's livelihoods, increase production, and enrich national strength on the one hand, and to enable students to develop outwards and manufacture goods to sell in foreign markets, especially in our country, as an important destination. For example, the fabrics dyed and woven by Kyoto Industrial School are the general-purpose printed cloth for our people, and the light bulbs manufactured are the general-purpose 200-volt long light bulbs used throughout our country, clearly marked for use by Chinese people. Students should strive to learn how to manufacture and sell them. After our visit, we couldn't help but feel terrified. Recently, various parties in our country have been advocating vocational education or life education, but many have not paid attention to the needs of society, the adequacy of equipment, and the training of teachers. This should be considered carefully. (To be continued)

Shandong Province Schools Will Change the Method of Paying Teachers: Salaries Will Be Paid Monthly Instead of Calculated by Clock Hours; The Education Department Convened a Meeting of Principals to Study 222

(Jinan Communication) The Ministry of Education previously issued a circular ordering schools in various provinces and cities to change the method of paying teachers' teaching salaries, prohibiting calculation by clock hours, and uniformly changing to monthly salaries. Previously, principals who held concurrent classes and received salaries will also be changed so that principals who hold concurrent classes for ten hours will not be paid. Many provinces are now implementing this, but because it is difficult to change suddenly in this province, it is still under consideration. The Ministry of Education is urging them to comply quickly. The Education Department has specially convened principals of provincial secondary schools and above to Shanghai to hold a meeting to study the implementation method. The meeting was held in the Education Department conference room at 9:00 AM today (the 9th). The attendees included Cai Fuyuan, the head of the First Normal School; Lin Shuyong, the principal of the Second Normal School; Wang Baolian, the principal of the First Women's Normal School; Qian Zhendong, the principal of the First Rural Normal School; Dong Fengchen, the principal of the Second Rural Normal School; Xiong Xiushan, the principal of the Fifth Rural Normal School; Chang Zizhong, the principal of the Sixth Rural Normal School; Song Huanwu, the principal of the High School; Meng Xianji, the principal of the First Vocational School; Ma Tingliang, the principal of the Second Vocational School; Wang Chaodong, the principal of the Third Vocational School; Hu Ganqing, the acting principal of the First Middle School; Hong Peiyuan, the principal of the Fourth Middle School; Yan Renpei, the principal of the Seventh Middle School; Su Jizhou, the principal of the First Women's Middle School; Sun Qingshan, the principal of the Twelfth

Middle School. The attendees from the Education Department included Wang Ziyu, the chief secretary; Liu Cipian, the secretary; Kong Lingcan, the head of the First Section; Qi Luxiang, the staff member; Lai Zhizhong, the head of the Second Section; Kong Eryi, the staff member; Zhang Zicai, the staff member; and Yang Mengyuan from the Audit Committee. Wang Ziyu presided over the meeting. During the discussion of the reform methods, it was decided to divide the review into four groups due to the many difficulties in suddenly reforming: the high school normal school group, the junior high school group, the vocational school group, and the rural normal school group. The principals will review in groups and present the review results for discussion at the Education Department at 9:00 AM tomorrow (the 10th).

Jiangsu Education Department Orders Zhenjiang County Education Bureau to Improve 223

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to Zhenjiang County Education Bureau, stating that according to investigation reports, the county's various social education institutions still have many areas that need improvement. These are listed separately as follows:

㈠ Modao Lane Public Education Center:

1. The center's premises are narrow, the light is dark, and the floor is damp, which is not suitable for use. Methods should be devised to improve this.

2. The purpose of livelihood surveys is to compare production quantity with consumption quantity. The center's livelihood surveys lack clear records of both production and consumption quantities. A detailed investigation should be conducted as soon as possible.

3. Illiterates in the basic education area account for one-half of the total population. According to statistical results, most of the illiterate are women. Future promotion of language education should pay attention to women.

4. The people in the area cannot sincerely accept various educations. This is because there are too few opportunities for contact on weekdays. In the future, methods should be devised to establish practical contact with the people.

5. Very few urban residents are physically strong, which is due to a lack of exercise opportunities. The original national martial arts training class in the center should be restored as soon as possible.

㈠ Baoyan Town Farmer Education Center:

1. Transportation in Baoyan is inconvenient, and news is delayed. The center plans to raise funds to install a wireless radio receiver, which should be implemented as soon as possible.

2. The existing charts in the center mostly contain statistics from various countries around the world. Statistical charts concerning this country, this province, this county, and this district are still lacking and should be added immediately.

3. Public schools should be held entirely within the basic education area to eliminate illiteracy.

4. The streets of Baoyan Town are dirty, which is detrimental to hygiene. A township improvement association should be organized as soon as possible, and local forces should be used to guide each household to clean diligently and to ban the free-range raising of livestock such as pigs and sheep.

5. There are occasional armed conflicts among the people. This trend should be jointly addressed and eliminated by local party and government agencies.

㈢ Huashan Farmer Education Center:

1. The center has been established for five years, and the director has been changed six times, resulting in a complete loss of public trust. Future work should start with the most important and urgent aspects for farmers in order to awaken public sympathy.

2. Low-lying fields are suitable for growing rice, and high-lying fields are suitable for growing miscellaneous grains. However, local farmers only like to grow rice, regardless of the height of the field, which not only results in a poor harvest, but sometimes no grain at all. Special attention should be paid to guiding the improvement of agricultural practices in the future.

3. The center's basic education area includes six villages, including Huashan, Tangcun, Shangshe, and Shiqiao, with 1,200 households and a population of approximately 5,000, which is too large and should be reduced immediately.

4. The 20 mu of public property in Pingchang City that local people previously designated should still be recovered for use as a model farm.

5. Most of the students in public schools are students from private schools who come here for remedial study, which is inconsistent with the original purpose of running public schools. The number of women in the daytime class is too small, and both should be improved.

The above points should be conveyed separately for improvement, and the progress of the improvement should be reported for review and order. This order.
