Shenbao National Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

Hurry Up and Protect Production Enterprises 230

— Natural

In this era of foreign goods dumping and rampant Japanese goods, the most unfortunate news is the frequent labor strikes in domestic goods factories over the past month, creating opportunities for the sales of foreign and Japanese goods, which is truly heartbreaking. However, the government is watching this situation as if it were a fire across the river, perfunctorily dealing with it, resulting in a situation that is getting worse and worse, inevitably leading to the closure and suspension of many factories. This is such a sad thing. In this helpless situation, I suddenly saw a public notice from Chairman Chiang, earnestly advocating the elimination of labor-capital disputes and the enrichment of production capacity. When workers go on strike for no reason, the competent authority may order the dissolution of the labor union to quickly resolve the issue, but factory owners are also not allowed to mistreat workers, and so on. This straightforward order is indeed a key way to protect production enterprises and resolve capital disputes. If the authorities of each province and city government can deeply understand Chairman Chiang's intentions and strictly enforce them, find ways to ban and suppress them, so that those who run factories can work with peace of mind, and the budding domestic goods industry can slowly develop, and can compete with foreign and Japanese goods. Otherwise, a glimmer of hope is also hopeless, and sooner or later China will be occupied by foreign and Japanese merchants. The China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association issued a notice yesterday endorsing Chairman Chiang's protection of production, stating that "Labor strikes are frequent, which is heartbreaking to say. In many cases, the matter is very small and can be resolved immediately, but it is only because there are people inciting behind the scenes that it often involves months and days. The crux of the matter is that every labor strike is controlled by a small number of manipulators and blackmailers, who use ignorant workers as a tool for their own use, resulting in a lose-lose situation. The factory is unable to support itself, and the workers also lose their livelihood, making future entrepreneurs see setting up a factory as a dangerous path and dare not try it rashly." These many painful and profound words, the general manipulating blackmailing in the middle sow the seeds of dissension of the elements, conscience fruit in, don't want to be the great sinners of national goods, also should suddenly realize, transfer the technique of inciting, come together to maintain the livelihood of the pitiable workers and support the endangered national goods industry. Perhaps China's national goods factory still has a place to exist. The general public will not be reduced to starvation. And those in charge of administration should also use a quick knife to cut through the mess to deal with this continuous labor tide as soon as possible, in order to maintain the only vitality of the place and the opportunity for workers' lives. This is what the reporter said with tears, and dares to pray for the national goods industry.

National Goods Talk

Talking about Current Affairs 231

— Ke Ding'an

The current affairs I want to talk about are the rampant "Modern Destruction Group." They are dedicated to destroying modern clothing, and their weapons of destruction are said to be "sprinkling sulfuric acid." This swift and thunderous method is enough to shock young men and women who like to be modern!

However, on closer thought, there are many illogical aspects to them! First, is the word "modern" reasonable? Second, do their executors have the ability to distinguish whether goods are domestic? Third, is sprinkling sulfuric acid reasonable? Fourth, is sulfuric acid a domestic product? Now, let's talk about these four points. First, "modern" means "contemporary," which is in line with modernization and is a very trendy thing, but it is not reprehensible. Second, there are many Chinese-made modern wool and silk fabrics. Even experts may find it difficult to distinguish them at a glance. I think that they, driven by momentary righteous indignation, certainly do not have the ability to distinguish them very well! If they think that something is modern and not a domestic product and destroy it, but that person is wearing clothes made of authentic domestic wool or silk, wouldn't they be wronged and suffer an unprovoked disaster? Third, it is said that sulfuric acid can not only destroy clothes, but also corrode the skin. Then, even if their clothes are modern foreign goods, it is inhumane for their bodies to be harmed for no reason, isn't it? Fourth, it is said that there is no sulfuric acid made in China yet! Then, they have already violated the tenet of "promoting domestic goods."

I think it is better to actively build than to passively destroy. How to build? I will contribute a little foolishness. Whether in each village or town, you can hold a "National Goods Consumption Association." Their responsibility is to "diligently persuade people to use domestic goods," starting from each member's family, then extending to relatives and friends, and then spreading from relatives and friends to relatives and friends, gradually reaching remote rural areas. There will be "National Goods Consumption Associations" everywhere. In this way, wouldn't there be no need for passive destruction? According to the plan of the China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association, in a few years, Chinese national goods companies can be seen everywhere in the country, which means that Chinese people can buy Chinese goods everywhere.

Also, destroying people's modern clothing in this way is in danger of violating criminal law. No wonder Director Wang wants to explicitly prohibit it!

Talking about the Modern Destruction Group 232

— Wang Shouqiu

Although the import of foreign goods has increased year by year, its sales path is entirely in large cities, and its patrons are entirely people in the intellectual community. Look at the modern men in suits and leather shoes, and the modern women with fluffy hair. Which one of them, from head to toe, is not a foreign product? But aren't they knowledgeable? Why don't they love the country like this? Alas! It's also pitiful to say! They are deeply poisoned by modernity! They think that they cannot be called modern if they don't do this. Modern, modern, you are really harmful!

According to a special telegram from Hangzhou published in the newspaper, "The Modern Destruction Group was discovered in Hangzhou City and appeared in various amusement venues every night. Western suits and women's foreign coats have been cut, affecting more than a thousand people." This is really a gratifying thing. The only way to deal with these people who only know how to be modern and don't know how to love the country is to use this method to deal with them. However, in terms of law, I am afraid it is illegal again. Therefore, this method can only be happy for a while, and should not be taken as an example. I think the best thing is to carve a few turtle seals and stamp them on anyone who wears foreign goods. And use indelible oil. Print it on them so that they can't wear it again. In this way, it may be possible to achieve some results in promoting national goods, which is much better than just shouting for promotion without actually doing it. Readers, what do you think?

Home Visit Record

Mrs. Cai Zimin 233

— Yu Qiacheng

I remember one snowy winter morning I visited Mr. Cai Zimin to ask about issues of youth cultivation. Now, on a chilly spring afternoon, I visited Mrs. Cai. Originally, Mrs. Cai Zhou Jun, had already expressed many opinions on the issue of national goods at meetings during this year of National Goods for Women. However, because we wanted to introduce every female leader who is engaged in promoting the national goods movement, and especially to introduce everyone's opinions on their work in the process of this work, I finally went to the west of Shanghai to pay my respects.

The guest room was very quiet, and the simple arrangement contained a sense of beauty. In front of the window and on the ground were scattered several potted plants that were in bloom. On the wall were several oil paintings accompanied by a six-foot-long portrait of Mr. Cai, and only one pair of five-character seal couplets by Mr. Wu Zhihui remained from the spring. The impression given to us here was not vulgarity with a lot of red and green, but another kind of elegance.

When Mrs. Cai walked in, she was wearing clothes made of domestic cloth, and her attitude was dignified and her speech was decisive and powerful.

We immediately talked about the Shanghai Women's National Goods Association, which was an organization that had been established many years ago. The members were housewives from intellectual families. Although many members have now gone to other places, Mrs. Cai, Mrs. Pan, Mrs. Li Haoran, and Mrs. Shen are still continuing their efforts. This association was organized before the Year of National Goods and the Year of National Goods for Women. The regulations and covenants were very strict, but Mrs. Cai has always adhered to them. When I asked how the Year of National Goods for Women could complete its great mission, Mrs. Cai replied, "In addition to the efforts of women to promote it, many things that relate to the overall situation need to be assisted and carried out by the state and society!"

"Because it is human nature to love cheapness, the fundamental solution is for the government to increase taxes on imported goods and at the same time reduce transit taxes on domestic products. This is much more effective than promoting domestic goods by mouth!" At the same time, to supplement the above reasons, she said with sadness and indignation, "Now Oriental goods are actually cheaper than domestic goods!"

Regarding the work of the Year of National Goods for Women, Mrs. Cai advocated adopting a persuasion approach. The current persuasion can only reach a relatively close part. The method of promotion should focus on activities in women's groups and girls' schools. For example, if a school has 100 female students who fully accept and agree with it, each person can persuade her own family, which is actually equivalent to persuading 100 families. At the time, she also talked about reaching out to female workers in factories. However, facts tell us that, due to economic reasons, it is mostly the intellectual class, the so-called upper class, who promote foreign goods. Therefore, she advocated that we should have a concept of ""it is shameful to use foreign goods, and it is respectable to use domestic goods even if they are not beautiful"", and build up such a public mentality!

Finally, Mrs. Cai summarized her opinions: 1. I hope that the government will raise tariffs on imported goods and engage in practical promotion of domestic goods from an economic perspective; 2. I hope that the industrial and commercial sectors will investigate domestic and imported goods separately so that those engaged in promotion will have reliable information; 3. In addition, women should work hard to do this during the Year of National Goods for Women. Only in this way is it possible to achieve success!

If you want to buy imported goods, go to a cooperative shop and ask!

National Goods Discussion

New Life Uniforms and National Goods 234

— Qian Zuizhu

The New Life Movement has been going on for only a month now, and its vigorous atmosphere has spread throughout the country. Its progress has also gradually moved from words to facts.

The covenants that stipulate the new life in terms of clothing, food, housing, and transportation have also been seen in newspapers. If they can be implemented accordingly, then there will be a brand new look in a short period of time, and the effect of changing customs and habits will be achieved.

However, there is one more thing that no one seems to have mentioned; and it is actually very necessary, which is…

"People engaged in the New Life should have a symbol – a uniform."

"The city likes high buns, and the four sides are one foot high." This is indeed the ironclad proof of "what those above like, those below will like even more"; but if those who like high buns only "like it in their hearts" and do not "comb a high bun" to show people, well, there will definitely not be a great effect of "four sides are one foot high" in a short period of time.

Assuming that we use "national material Zhongshan suits" as the uniform for people engaged in the New Life Movement, then there are at least the following benefits.

First, wearing a uniform requires one to restrain one's actions at all times and arouse a sense of self-esteem; at least, one does not dare to be romantic, dirty, or frivolous, because one is being watched.

Second, demonstrate to others and arouse the admiration of society, and think about imitating and reforming. At least, make those who do not wear uniforms (i.e., those who do not lead a new life) feel ashamed and reflect inwardly.

Third, domestic goods can sell well, because there is a uniform everywhere that restrains his actions and reminds his conscience. At least, domestic cloth and silk can be popular, and foreign goods can not be bought. Fourth, the spirit of cleanliness and simplicity can be fully expressed in the uniform; one can monitor each other's words and deeds to see if they are "practicing the New Life"; one can give society a fresh impression and make the New Life Movement advance faster.

If it is not stipulated that "people in the New Life must wear uniforms," then the benefits mentioned above will become harm. For example, the first item above becomes…

"Not wearing a uniform, there is no need to restrain one's hands, and it will not arouse a sense of self-esteem. You can still be romantic... because you are not being watched."

Wouldn't this kind of New Life that is not responsible for others or oneself be loose and empty?

Therefore, to promote domestic goods, we must vigorously implement the New Life, and to vigorously implement the New Life, we must stipulate the use of uniforms. These three things seem to be unrelated, but in fact they are interlinked.

What year is it for these tasteless things?

A Few Points to Eliminate Hatred of Goods 236

— Diao

"Promoting National Goods" and "Consuming National Goods" are resounding slogans that are making a lot of noise; but I ask you, is the hatred of foreign goods completely eliminated? Are modern girls using them? I can conclude that with this kind of high-profile promotion, foreign goods are still being imported like sweat.

What do you mean by high-profile promotion? It means that on the surface, people are very enthusiastic, but in secret they are the biggest customers of foreign goods. With this kind of promotion, can foreign goods not disappear? If you want them to disappear, you must do the following.

1. Set an example… Dr. Shao Shuangqiu, when he promoted the local goods movement, he actually "set an example" by wearing local goods, just like a worker. When he went out to visit and give speeches, even if he was looked down upon, his spirit did not diminish. I hope that the concubines and young ladies of the current authorities and the leaders of all sectors can all be like Dr. Shao, "set an example", and guarantee that unscrupulous merchants will sell foreign goods? If it can be implemented, I think a group of compatriots will definitely use them, and will never have the face to sell them again, right?

2. Abandon the concept of foreign goods… When using domestic goods for the first time, there must be some modern people who are still reluctant to part with foreign goods and do not want to use domestic goods; because domestic goods are not as gorgeous as foreign goods, and they want to reduce their beautiful appearance. "You must know that domestic goods have the beauty of domestic goods, and foreign goods have the beauty of foreign goods." You must never have the concept that foreign goods must be beautiful. I hope that first-time users will quickly abandon this concept, or else how can they universally "consume domestic goods"?

3. Cheap domestic goods… When "promoting domestic goods", I hope that national goods merchants will sell them at a low price as soon as possible, and never worry about losing money; the sacrifice now is the development in the future. Because we want to make a group of people especially cheap when they are transitioning to "consuming domestic goods", and improve the goods; in this way, I think we can get a group of people to like to buy domestic goods.

The above points are also old sayings, but if you compatriots can do this, the great effect it will have will definitely be great.

Successful People in the National Goods Industry

In Memory of a Practitioner of Promoting National Goods 237

— Sun Choucheng

Mr. Xiang Songmao, the general manager of the Five Continents Pharmacy, showed extraordinary intelligence from a young age, different from ordinary people. Growing up with great aspirations, he was forced by circumstances to abandon his studies and learn commerce. During his free time, he always had a book in hand, studying diligently. He inscribed a long couplet as his motto, which read, "In ordinary times, one should restrain desires to nourish the body, but in times of great adversity, one should accept fate and sacrifice life," and "In managing a family, one must live within one's means, but for the sake of righteousness, one should regard thousands of gold as insignificant." His selflessness is evident from this. After taking charge of Five Continents, he personally attended to every matter, never complaining about hardship or resentment. He once went to Japan to inspect the pharmaceutical industry. After returning to China, he purchased land to establish the Gubeng Soap Factory, Yalin Medicated Water Factory, and Dongwu Cotton Factory, hiring specialized personnel to research various products. He believed that relying on selling foreign goods resulted in the outflow of profits and rights. Therefore, it was necessary to invent new medicines oneself to benefit patients and prevent the loss of national wealth. He promoted national goods not with empty talk but with practical action. Therefore, the Shanghai National Goods Factory Joint Association elected him as an executive committee member. In every meeting, his insightful opinions always hit the mark, winning the respect and admiration of everyone, who honored him as a practitioner of promoting national goods. After the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, Mr. Xiang was filled with righteous indignation and planned strategies to resist the invaders. He organized a volunteer army within the factory, training them day and night, and joined the boycott of enemy goods organizations, actively working. During the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the Five Continents' second branch on Kaozha Road was searched by the enemy, and eleven employees, including Jiang Bangyu, Yu Gengfeng, Tong Yongcai, Qi Dejiang, Ding Zhaonian, Xu Zhijie, Chen Hankun, Wu Chenliang, Li Shengcai, Zhou Ruilong, and Tao Fu, were arrested, their fates unknown. Upon hearing the news, Mr. Xiang personally went to rescue them. His colleagues tried to dissuade him, but Mr. Xiang said, "As the company manager, this concerns the lives of eleven people. How can I not enter the tiger's den to save them?" He then ventured forth at great risk. He returned safely the first time, but was arrested on his second attempt. Seeing his business card, the enemy escorted him to the headquarters of the Marine Corps, questioning him about the reasons for organizing the volunteer army and boycotting Japanese goods. It turned out that the enemy had long been wary of him and taken note of him. Mr. Xiang spoke frankly, stating that the enemy should not disregard international conventions by forcibly occupying our land and massacring our compatriots. The enemy, angered by his unyielding stance, harmed him. This happened on January 31st, 1932. Unyielding in the face of force, he died a martyr, bringing glory to the nation. Though dead, he lived on. Therefore, the factory colleagues all engraved the three characters "131" on their badges to commemorate their grief. Recently, the factory planned to publish a special issue titled "In Memory of Mr. Xiang Songmao," inviting Supervisory Committee member Gao Youtang to write Mr. Xiang's biography. The manuscript has already been completed and contains phrases such as, "If Songmao had been wise and protected himself, not resisted Japan or rejected Japanese goods, he could have lived; not rescued people or taken risks, he could have lived; if he had knelt and begged for mercy from the Japanese invaders, willing to submit and be humiliated, he could have lived. But Songmao ultimately died for resisting Japan, rejecting Japanese goods, rescuing people, taking risks, and refusing to submit or be humiliated. Sima Qian said, 'Death can be heavier than Mount Tai.' This is what he meant by Songmao. With Songmao's death, Songmao became immortal. How can Songmao be said to have died?" Such words are enough to inspire spirits and encourage those who follow. Therefore, this is specially highlighted to inform my comrades who are enthusiastic about promoting national goods and concerned about national affairs.

National Goods Drama

The Power of Influence 238

— Sai Yu

Time: Some afternoon.

Location: A very wide road, but not crowded with people.

Characters: A vendor shouting along the road, Father, Son.

Setting: The father is leading the son by the hand, approaching from a distance. There is a vendor over there, holding small toy cars in his hand, shouting loudly, hoping to attract some customers, but there are none.

Vendor: Toy cars, want toy cars? Six copper coins to ride to the Bund!

Son: (Stops and refuses to move forward.) Daddy... this toy car is very fun. Let's buy one too!

Father: (Asks the vendor) How much does one of these cars cost?

Vendor: Only six copper coins! Look, isn't it very small and cute? (Takes one out and shows it off to them.)

Father: (Takes the car, looking at it repeatedly from all angles. Suddenly shows a surprised expression.) This thing isn't a national product, is it? (To son) We shouldn't buy this thing. Let's go buy one made by Chinese people instead!

Vendor: (Smiling) Aren't foreign goods the same, sir?

Father: (Slightly angry) You! Why don't you sell things made by Chinese people, and insist on selling foreign goods?

Son: This thing is a foreign product? We don't want to buy it then. I always hear our teacher at school say... we Chinese people should buy Chinese goods.

Father: (With a sincere attitude towards the vendor) I advise you to give up selling this kind of goods and sell national goods instead!

Vendor: Sir! We just want to get some profit. What do we care about national goods or foreign goods?

Son: (Shows an impatient expression) Let's go! Don't talk to him anymore.

Father: (While stopping his son from going forward, speaks to the vendor very sincerely) Don't you always hope that your own family will prosper? That's because you are a member of the family, and after the family prospers, you can also benefit. The nation is like a big family, and you and I are all members of this big family. If the big family can become strong, then we, as members of the family, can also benefit. But to make our big family strong, we must first do the work of strengthening the nation. If you can promote national goods, that is one way to strengthen our big family. Do you understand this reason?

Vendor: Sir! What you said is certainly right, but I don't know if selling Chinese goods is easy or not?

Father: Of course, you use the same method as selling foreign goods. After you sell your current stock, you can then promote national goods, and I hope you persuade your colleagues as well. Then, you will have made a great effort for the big family. (To son) Let's go!

The Year of National Goods, Bound by Red Thread 239

— Zhang Mengzhao

Bright spring sunshine! Replacing the withered, harsh winter! The plums and apricots are blooming in competition, and the green grass is like a carpet. "Spring slumber unaware of the dawn, everywhere one hears the song of birds." What a lovely season this is!

Sanbao, a self-reliant woman, is wearing a spring dress of apple green color made by the Meiya Silk Factory! Her collar is tied with a silk embroidered handkerchief of national goods! Her feet are wearing white canvas rubber-soled shoes from the Chen Jiageng Company! She especially shows off her willow eyebrows, almond eyes, and graceful figure as a beautiful woman!

Her name, Sanbao (Three Treasures), is derived from her love for the three practical national goods. These three treasures were given to her by her lover, Mr. S.

Mr. S does not propose to Sanbao. He thinks; the passionate love between a man and woman should not be forced, it should be allowed to develop naturally! She sees the objects (the three national goods) and thinks of the person! Perhaps she will fall in love with me! She also feels that Mr. S is a likable person. She thinks he does not pursue the opposite sex with small favors, but is generous and loves the country, loves national goods, and loves the loved one! It is such bliss to be his life companion! How can she miss this opportunity?

Without seeking his consent, on this bright spring day, a large advertisement appeared in the newspaper, a marriage announcement of Sanbao and Mr. S. Relatives and friends were surprised and said, "The Year of National Goods, Bound by Red Thread!" This is a beautiful story about Sanbao!

Chinese Inventors Invent New Style Condensed Milk Machine 240

The West Lake Condensed Milk Company was founded by Xiao Jiagan. Diligently managed, it has been seven years since, and the business is becoming increasingly prosperous. The Yanchai brand condensed milk produced is in greater demand than supply. Recently, Mr. Xiao invented a milk powder machine, and the products are excellent. He has applied to the Ministry of Industry for a ten-year patent, named "Roller Vacuum Combined Type." In addition, there is also the invention of a condensed milk air compressor. This machine uses a certain gas to compress the air out of the condensed milk can, so that the color and taste of the condensed milk inside the can remain unchanged for a long time. This invention is the first of its kind in our country and has attracted the attention of all sectors of society. Mr. Zhang Jingjiang, chairman of the National Government's Construction Committee, also believes that it is a promising creative undertaking in our country and has joined the founders to show his approval. Shanghai banking circles such as the Bank of Communications and Zhejiang Industrial Bank have all agreed to provide strong support. It is said that the company believes that the import of dairy products in recent years has reached 20 million yuan, and milk powder is the most. Moreover, the tariffs are very heavy, with more than 48 yuan in national currency levied per morning kilogram, which is the best opportunity to recover profit rights. Therefore, the company has decided to expand ordinary shares to 120,000 yuan in addition to the full subscription, and plans to publicly add 80,000 yuan of preferred shares. According to Mr. Xiao, the company currently has more than 200 dairy cows and more than 2,000 acres of pasture. There is absolutely no problem with expanding the pasture, and there is also great confidence in the manufacturing side. The company can manufacture all dairy products from various countries, and the machines manufactured are all designed by Mr. Xiao. It is said that the total cost of all machines will be less than 40,000 yuan. If they are custom-made from abroad, it will cost at least tens of thousands of yuan, and the mechanical capacity may be higher than that of foreign goods. Among them, a single-effect vacuum machine can reach a vacuum degree of more than 30 degrees, which has broken the world vacuum record. For the sake of advanced study, Mr. Xiao is now exploring the principle of high altitude. If he can get what he wants, the world's vacuum meter will not be limited to 30 degrees in the future, and there will be a high-altitude vacuum meter to replace it.

On Domestic Tonics 242

— Shu

Among the valuable domestic tonics, the first is Jilin ginseng, and the second is Sichuan white fungus. However, truly wild ginseng is very rare, and most of it is produced by artificial cultivation. It is extremely difficult to distinguish between the superior and the inferior. Speaking of its efficacy, it only refreshes the mind and invigorates qi, which is what Western medicine calls containing excitatory substances. A previous report stated that a certain Mr. Zhang in Zhabei, Shanghai, bought and ate 20 yuan of ginseng, which resulted in his sudden death. Western medicine diagnosed that it was caused by excessive excitement from eating ginseng. This is like adding fuel to the fire, increasing its flames. Moreover, the ultimate element of any part of the human body that ginseng possesses has not been scientifically verified in this era of scientific advancement. In the end, it is difficult for everyone to take it with peace of mind. Now that the producing area of ginseng has fallen to a strong neighbor, I am even more unwilling to eat it to provide funds for the enemy. Therefore, most Chinese people have changed to eating Sichuan white fungus. Because the Sichuan white fungus has been sold exclusively by the Sichuan store in the local Paoqiu field for many years. The number of eaters is increasing day by day, the sales are booming, and the efficacy is also greatly enhanced. Such as male and female yin deficiency, physical weakness, blood deficiency, lung disease, hemorrhoids, women's irregular menstruation, children's physical weakness, buying and eating the store's white fungus have significant effects. The owner of the store believes that Sichuan white fungus has such great efficacy and has occupied the primary position of domestic tonics. And in view of the customs records of the import of foreign medicines every year, there are tens of millions of dollars, most of which are proprietary medicines and tonics that do not meet the constitution of the Chinese people. Both the leak of national wealth is alarming and the obstruction of health is difficult. Sichuan white fungus has been trusted by the Chinese people. Without scientific chemical verification, it is important to deeply understand what tonic elements it contains, so that the Chinese people have a deeper understanding of Sichuan white fungus. Everyone should work hard to promote it in order to reduce the invasion of imported tonics. In 1931, a huge amount of Sichuan white fungus was requested by Hu Zejun of the Chinese Science Society for precise scientific chemical verification. As a result, Sichuan white fungus, in addition to containing potassium, iron, sulfur, sodium, fat, protein, and other elements, produced a large amount of mucilage similar to gum arabic in the water-boiled solution. In summary, the various tonic elements contained have the following major functions. 1. Replenish blood. 2. Help digestion. 3. Benefit bowel movements. With the Sichuan white fungus alone, it has three major effects, which is truly unmatched by any tonic. Although Sichuan stores are in the midst of a depression in the Shanghai market, the store's business has grown year by year. The breadth of its sales can also be seen.

Free Talk

The Characteristics of the Chinese People 243

— Ana

Social practices like bowing, hand-cupping salutations, and kowtowing are not habits that should exist in modern times, but rather remnants of the "prosperous past." Northerners are more servile than Southerners because they are closer to the imperial capital and have been subject to traditional oppression... The Manchus were adept at hand-cupping salutations, and the "Beijing style" officialdom was very strong, which is an example.

The blame for this should be placed squarely on Shusun Tong. He lacked ambition and was unable to express himself, so he created elaborate "court rituals" to please Emperor Gaozu of Han, making him the epitome of a lackey. In this 20th-century era of freedom and equality, lackeys should repent and reform. In America, the arrogance of the president or high officials is far less than that of a small magistrate or "master" in our country. This is simply because they are civilized and democratic, while we are not. They are getting things done, while we are causing trouble...

However, the human spirit has always been free. No matter how much it is subjected to the education of lackeys, its nature still desires freedom. Many petty officials are consumed by their desires, wanting to become high officials, precisely because they are still oppressed when they are petty officials, and can be more free when they are high officials. No one has ever been willing to be oppressed, or felt comfortable being used as a brick embedded in a wall. But since they are bricks, they cannot escape the confines of the wall, so they only want to oppress their colleagues, wanting to be the brick on top, with all the weight below them and no higher oppression, in other words, being more free.

With the change in the economic system, the situation is different. Having money means being more free. This is the development of commercial society. No matter how much one is looked down upon, scolded, or oppressed, becoming a tycoon can transform one into an "important person" or "celebrity." At that time, one will not be oppressed, can retaliate against oppressors, and can manipulate many things, like an emperor. So people bow their heads and lower their eyes, letting others laugh and scold, whether for officials or merchants, all aiming to make money, as if they have grasped the main vein, becoming gold miners.

People in the "thirty-six trades" and "seventy-two trades" of society are simply educating themselves, educating their children, and educating others in this way. Some say that three ordinary Europeans are not as good as one Jew, and three Jews are not as good as one Chinese person. There is truth to this saying. China is traditionally oppressed, acting as a lackey while also wanting to be the master, all struggling in bitterness! Striving to be hardworking, ruthless, and stingy towards oneself! Also ruthless, stingy, and cruel towards others.

"A Way Out" 244

— Peng Xuezhen

I just came back from seeing off a friend at the station. Walking down Pingmen Bridge, my umbrella touched someone else's umbrella. I looked up:

Under that tattered oiled paper umbrella, the mother and daughter, Little Beizi, were both speaking in a sharp voice...

"Oh!" Both of their arrowhead-colored faces wore bitter smiles.

Without them saying anything, I suddenly remembered that Little Beizi was going to Shanghai today. She had told me this last night while drawing well water. This girl had a winter vacation, and every night she went to my place to learn a few characters. Her deep and dark eyes revealed her intelligence. Now she can write the songs she usually recites on paper.

Yesterday Little Beizi told me she was going to Shanghai, and I thought she was joking. At this moment, I unconsciously turned around and walked towards the station with them again.

"It is a proper place to eat, after all. Little Beizi's godmother introduced her. She said that her voice is clear and soft, and she's very good at learning to sing Qing opera, 呃, she's just singing songs, and doesn't..." Her mother breathed a sigh of relief. "There's nothing else she can do, her father owes money, and doesn't even have money to buy silkworm eggs."

"She's still young, isn't she, fifteen?" "Sixteen, a flower-like age! Getting a little money to make ends meet."

The woman said it quite frankly, but the tightly locked brow told people that her heart, like that tattered oiled paper umbrella, had countless holes.

Little Beizi remained silent throughout, as if she were enduring and choking back the bitter water of life. I thought of her quick wit and clear singing voice across the river on summer nights.

For this little bit of talent, Little Beizi found "a way out."

On the platform, the bell rang rapidly three times. Little Beizi stepped silently onto the train, tears welling up in the corners of her eyes.

"Go well, your godmother will pick you up at the Shanghai station."

The engine spewed ink-dragon-like smoke, and the tracks rumbled.

Little Beizi's mother sobbed as she walked out of the tunnel with me.

The light rain continued to fall relentlessly. We held up our umbrellas and walked silently on the stone path, carrying the same heavy heart.

I secretly estimated... Little Beizi washing her face clean, applying a little rouge, and putting on a simple cheongsam, would be a pitifully attractive courtesan!

By the Banks of the Wenlan Bridge 245

— Ms. Cao Ming

The Wenlan Bridge is a white stone bridge with iron railings in my hometown. It crosses the small river that surrounds the east of the village.

On this side of the village is the coal bunker and pond at the bottom of the Zhongxinheng Silk Factory. On the opposite bank are two rows of mulberry trees lining the road as far as the eye can see, and beyond that are vegetable fields and fish ponds. In the summer, that is where the farmers rest after dinner. Many people gather on this bridge, each talking about their daytime activities and simple feelings. Men lean against the railings, and women, pestered by children, sit on the stone steps holding their water pipes.

Each Generation is Better than the Last 246

— Zang Kejia

丨Random Notes from a Windowless Room, Number Four

"Each generation is worse than the last"! This sentence has become a deterministic view of China's future in the eyes of most people. In fact, it is a vicious sarcastic remark. From a positive perspective, we should say, "Each generation is better than the last."

"Each generation is worse than the last" is a pessimistic view. If we calmly look forward, we can clearly see the reverse of this statement in both major and minor matters丨"Each generation is better than the last."

People of the previous generation have had their minds shaped by the past era, and no amount of whipping can move them forward. Hoping that they will get better is like hoping for a dying person. It's impossible. Who has the power to turn back the past? This era ultimately belongs to the future, and the people in this era are ultimately different from the previous generation. I once asked a young nun for her opinion on ghosts and gods. She said, "What ghosts and gods? I only have food to eat because I chant scriptures. I say there are ghosts and gods with my mouth." This answer is very frank. She approves of a married monk, saying that it is right. Judging from these words, she will definitely liberate herself if she has the opportunity.

If you give elementary and middle school students the topic "Your future aspirations," they will definitely say that they want to be revolutionaries, overthrow imperialism, overthrow warlords, overthrow..., and create a world of great harmony. There is no falsehood in this statement, because elementary school students don't know how to be false. I once saw an essay by a student from a railway primary school on this topic. He said that he wanted to be a section chief in the future. This shows that the young heart is always pure and white.

Some people have regarded "kill all those over thirty" as a terrifying slogan. Yes, this statement is a bit too extreme. However, expecting the people of the previous generation to make the world a better place is truly foolish and delusional! Putting hope in the hands of the next generation will definitely yield results, although the size of the fruit cannot be predicted.

He lazily sits on the broken steps,

Silently reading the spring sun

Sliding over his curved shoulders.

Looking at that purple-black hillside,

He sadly raised

The face deeply hidden in his hands.

Can no longer call back

The fields that belonged to someone else long ago?

He lazily sits on the broken steps,

Silently reading the spring sun

Sliding over his curved shoulders.

Random Thoughts on a Trip to Hangzhou 248

— Xu Maoyong

Having traveled to Hangzhou, I wanted to write a travelogue, but I felt there was nothing to write about; Hangzhou didn't give me any good material. However, I can't blame Hangzhou; I should blame myself... Traveling to Hangzhou shouldn't start from Shanghai in the first place.

If I had started from a remote countryside, arriving in Hangzhou would definitely be quite a sight. However, people departing from Shanghai always carry Shanghai in their hearts, and Hangzhou is striving to become Shanghai. This gives Shanghai tourists a sense of "having seen the great ocean" and "having seen the Wushan mountains," making Hangzhou seem "hard to be water" and "not like clouds."

Take the rickshaw, for example. Shanghai rickshaw pullers can navigate even the most crowded streets with ease and composure. If there's an obstacle, they simply shout "Hey!" as a warning. In Hangzhou, however, even on streets with few pedestrians, the rickshaw pullers are constantly shouting "Hey, keep to the side! Keep to the side!" and some other words I don't understand, appearing very flustered and rushed. Also, the entrances of Hangzhou hotels are often filled with rickshaws and pullers, making it almost impossible for others to pass, but the people of Hangzhou seem indifferent, and those who come to Hangzhou can do nothing about it. I believe that the nature of the city of Hangzhou is partly reflected in the rickshaws... It lacks order, but it doesn't really need much strict order. Because life in Hangzhou is not very tense in the first place; it's usually leisurely. On normal days, the pullers shouting "Keep to the side!" or something else is actually an expression of leisure.

Because they are used to leisure, Hangzhou inevitably becomes flustered and unable to maintain order when it comes to special, tense times. During the few days I was in Hangzhou, it was precisely such a tense time for the city. One reason was the pilgrimage season, when pious men and women came to pay their respects; the second was the spring break, when school teachers and students came for sightseeing; and the third was the period when the Zhejiang Province Boy Scouts were gathering in the provincial capital for a review.

The people of Hangzhou were flustered and rushed, but very happy, because this was an opportunity to make money. This year's business all depended on these few days. So, needless to say, hotel prices went up, restaurant prices went up, boat prices went up, rickshaw prices went up... everything went up. And the way they went up was truly frightening.

One evening, I was eating in a restaurant and saw a customer three or four tables away ordering sweet and sour fish, which is a famous Hangzhou dish. When the sweet and sour fish was ready, a waiter took it to another waiter, telling him to pass it to the customer, and at the same time instructed:

"Five jiao eight or six jiao four, you can calculate it yourself."

Because they were speaking right next to me, I heard it very clearly and was a little surprised.

That day happened to be Qingming Festival, probably the busiest day in Hangzhou.

Two days later, the hustle and bustle had subsided a bit, and I also wanted to eat sweet and sour fish. So I went to the same restaurant and first asked the waiter about the price, which he said was four jiao eight.

When it arrived, the quality was the same as the "five jiao eight" or "six jiao four" from that day. I couldn't help but wonder if the customer that day had paid "five jiao eight" or "six jiao four"?

Things like this made the prices in Hangzhou at that time absurdly astonishing.

At that time, I had not yet reached the age of understanding things like adults, and I didn't quite understand their conversations. However, those talkative people often appeared in my memory, especially Wu Daniu, who was taller and more straightforward than anyone else.

He was a man of about thirty who didn't talk much but was willing to work. He had a nature that wouldn't yield even if a knife was swung at him—a nature often found in kind farmers. Standing next to him was like standing next to a solid, proudly upright cypress tree. He worked as a long-term laborer at the home of one of our wealthy uncles—Uncle Yonglu. In the morning, he carried basket after basket of mulberry leaves picked by the female workers to the market; he moved the "silkworm beds" among the adult women and thirteen- or fourteen-year-old children who were busy selecting mature silkworms. In addition, he had to irrigate the mulberry fields in the morning and evening and help with Uncle Yonglu's trivial household chores. "Well, this is how my hired hand should be. Be diligent, Daniu!" When silkworm farming was at its busiest, Uncle Yonglu would often say encouragingly to Daniu. In order to advocate using cheap prices to buy unexpected labor, he loved to say to people in a greedy tone... "Actually, everyone in the world should become as obedient and hardworking as oxen. As long as a few people take the lead. Look, if there are too many smart people, won't the world get worse and worse?"

The strong man was not tempted by the landlord's praise. He seemed to work only for fate, but sometimes when it exceeded his endurance, he would use more gloomy and clumsy movements to express his doubts; this aroused contempt and anger in the landlord. (To be continued)

Across the river, I see a forest of flowers,

Half a Day's Lesson (9) 251

— Li Huiying

The weather in early autumn is like intentionally playing jokes on people. In the morning, it spreads a light chill, but by noon, it can even bring out sunlight that is more unbearable than summer. The climate changes greatly within a single day. There is no wind, only the evaporation of heat. After three hours, I saw almost everyone's face dripping with sweat, but they, like me, forgot to wipe it with a handkerchief. Their entire mind and spirit seemed to be occupied by the depression inside.

Suddenly, someone on the stage started shouting:

"Long live the Great Japanese Empire!"

"Long live the Great Manchurian Empire!"

The crowd below followed, shouting in a chaotic noise like a big quarrel. Then, people were made to get on cars under the protection of police and soldiers and drove away.

A parade began. The route was to leave the sports field, walk along Shangyi Street, then Liangmihang Street, to the Governor's Office, then back to Liangmihang Street, Xinkaimen Street, out of Xinkaimen, along the main road to Laoti Fasi, turn into Chalu Kou Chaoyang Street, enter Dadongmen Henan Street, and return to the sports field to disband. The order of the parade was: military police in front, followed by Japanese elementary schools, Tongwen Commercial School, First Normal School, First Middle School, Girls' Middle School, Girls' Normal School, First Middle School, County Middle School, Midwifery School, Municipal Elementary School, County Elementary School. The sea of people surged, police whistles blew, people shouted and screamed, running around in chaos. A huge commotion broke out throughout the entire sports field.

It seemed I heard that this was a citizens' celebration, but apart from the students, not a single small citizen could be found in the procession. A large flag was being carried in front, a military band was playing music, and the crowd moved slowly. We were just playing the role of clowns in a drama.

Arriving at the Governor's Office, it turned out we were to shout "Long live" to Xi Qia three times! Facing the clear and mirror-like Songhua River beside me, and then thinking of the steep mountains and high peaks of Jiangnan, I thought to myself, how could the beautiful mountains and clear waters of Jilin, such a good land in Northeast China, be permanently occupied by Japanese imperialism! How could our thirty million people quietly be doing as slaves of a conquered nation, allowing our children and grandchildren to never be able to turn over! Oh, I cannot believe it!

In the clear sky, there were a few thin white clouds. The river breeze drifted by, warm and gentle. Who wouldn't say it was a good autumn day! However, on this day a year ago, and on the days after two years ago, wasn't a hideous farce and a cruel massacre being staged in Northeast China?

Turning back onto Liangmihang Street, I saw the brand-new signboard of "Xiehe Bookstore." (This was formerly the Zhonghua Bookstore, renamed by order of the Department of Education.) I thought to myself that in a few years, we probably wouldn't even be able to see the characters "Zhonghua."

The people in the procession gradually decreased. When I noticed some students secretly slipping out of the procession, I, who was already tired and reluctant to move my feet, also found an opportunity to slip to the outside of the procession and hide in a small alley on the side of the street.

It was already twelve o'clock.

"Half a day's lesson is considered done."

Thinking this, I slowly walked on the road home...

"When will we not have to take such lessons? When will we be able to regain our freedom?..." (The End)

Despite Rising Financial Silver Prices, the Standard Gold Market Remains Steady, with a Slight Drop of Three Jiao After an Initial Increase 252

The gold market was quite stable yesterday. Swap rates were nearing parity, and sentiment was relatively good. However, telegrams regarding the silver case were profit-driven, making it difficult for prices to rise sharply. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw both the U.S. and British markets rise in unison. The five-metal exchange saw forward silver prices increase by five hao to one and a half li, but the January contracts remained unchanged. Exchange rates narrowed, U.S. cotton rose by ten pounds, U.S. wheat rose by three and seven-five, and London spot gold rose by three pence, indicating a better overall environment. As a result, although the opening price of the gross market fell, it did not break the 50 yuan mark. Gan Changxiang Heng Yufu Xingyong competed to purchase, causing the price to rebound to above three yuan and a half. A Reuters report stated that the U.S. Senate subcommittee reported yesterday that the Agricultural Committee was scheduled to meet today to consider the Sires Silver Act and formally report to the Senate, with a vote possible within the week without delay. The report also mentioned the amendments by Weller and Thomas (three items omitted), causing prices to drop. However, Hui Xiang continued to advance and partially recovered. Later, Reuters reported again that the Sires Silver Act had a favorable situation within the Agricultural Committee, and that the Thomas Amendment, which would nationalize silver, was also gaining traction. This caused sentiment to turn cautious, and prices fell again after the opening. The Central Bank opened with over two hundred bars, and major players also bought heavily, stabilizing the market and causing it to hover around two yuan with little change. The price of red gold was estimated at 965 yuan. Because the swap premium for refined gold was feared to be high, many sellers emerged (those holding spot goods hedged with futures). The Central Bank's opening price also tended to be weak. The three-way swap, coinciding with the week, started early at 10 a.m. on Saturday. The market situation for the first half of the day is recorded as follows:

The opening price in the morning was 952 yuan and eight jiao, up three jiao compared to the previous close. Physical goods opened at the same price. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

The Noteworthy Kang-Tibetan Problem 271

— Hai Ru

In order to attempt to resolve their own and each other’s contradictions, the imperialists cannot but redistribute the markets and implement a forcible redivision of the colonies. China, a semi-colonial country, is currently in a situation of being divided and dominated by the imperialists. Since the September 18th Incident, Japanese imperialists have successively seized our four northeastern provinces, and the division has already begun. Now, the Kang-Tibetan problem in the western border region has followed the northeastern problem. Undoubtedly, the invasion of the Sichuan-Kang region by Tibetan troops is a clear manifestation of the British imperialists’ desire to implement a forcible division of China.

Our country’s people seem to have an excessively narrow perspective. They only know about Japan and only know about the Northeast, and most of them indifferently view the border issues in the western region. In this way, the British imperialists will be able to further invade our country’s western border region, and take the opportunity of our people not having time to look west, to bring the western provinces into their grasp, which is also within their expectations. In the past, such as Annam becoming French, and Burma belonging to the British, wasn’t it the same situation?

The authorities have always paid little attention to the Kang-Tibetan problem, nor have they had the opportunity to pay attention. The so-called “Kang-Tibetan Reorganization Plan,” “Serious Negotiations with the British,” etc., are just like empty talk on paper, and have no effect at all. Recently, such as the telegram from Liu Wenhui, the commander-in-chief of Sichuan and Kang, asking for assistance, requesting the government to provide powerful assistance, but what kind of assistance will the government provide besides issuing a telegram ordering resistance? Perhaps this is beyond the reach of the whip?

It is inevitable that Liu Wenhui cannot resist the Tibetan troops under the command and utilization of the British imperialists. Recently, according to a report in the Chongqing Xinmin Daily, the Kang-Tibetan situation has eased, and the Kang side has also sent Jiang Yuwen as a representative to negotiate with the Tibetan side. This clearly shows that Liu Wenhui is helpless due to lack of assistance, so he compromised, so that the long-term resistance could not but change to short-term resistance, and then from short-term resistance to "peaceful resistance." However, the British imperialists' active armed invasion of Xikang will not end because of Liu Wenhui's compromise. On the contrary, the more "peaceful resistance" there is, the more it will promote the active invasion of Tibetan troops. As a result, the entire Xikang province will fall into the hands of the British.

The fact is indeed like this... According to a report in the Chengdu March 27th Minshi Daily... "The news of the Tibetan bandits invading the Jinsha River has been repeatedly disclosed in previous reports. Recently, they have shown their stubborn means, thinking of ways to implement their policy of aggression, regardless of their lives

Financial resources, actively invade incessantly. It is also heard that the pro-British Galun Lingrongxian is advocating the use of force to seize the lost land, and declares that if

If the war is defeated, would rather be a vassal of England than seek peace with the Han people..." The Chengdu Xinxin News also reported... "The Kang-Tibetan war is about to expand, and Tibetan troops are strengthening their support by crossing the Jinsha River. The talk of peace is now hopeless." (March 26th)

Chengdu is located in the west and close to Xikang, so these news, needless to say, are absolutely true. The British are striving for Xikang, not because of reconciliation and compromise, just as the Japanese are striving for the Northeast, not because of the non-resistance and not knowing to be grateful and stop moving forward. For the armed aggression of the imperialists against weak nations, only force can respond to force, an eye for an eye, blood for blood. This is the attitude that China should have today.

The Kang-Tibetan problem is becoming increasingly serious. I hope the people of the whole country will pay more attention to it!

Women Who Are Like Children Appeal for Peace 272

— Chen

The war demon has been hovering in the sky for a long time, covering this magnificent land with a bleak shadow, foreshadowing the destruction of countless human lives under its bloody kiss. The traces of blood from the previous decade have not yet disappeared, and an even greater storm is about to rise, which has prompted humanitarians who cherish "compassion" to appeal for peace, making a big splash, while the cowardly and weak people are at a loss, crying incessantly. Recently, French women, amidst this sorrow and helplessness, have joined the "World Women's League" to promote the world peace movement, which is this manifestation. We see it in their "Church World Friendship Alliance," friends of Gandhi, and the International Women's Association, listed in the petition to the powerful church leaders of various countries, stating... "We, as the mothers of children, the children of the world are our children, how can we sit idly by and watch our children slaughter each other without lending a hand?" Almost every word is a tear. Then, such as "The world has entered a dangerous period. We, in the name of innocent children, and in the name of mothers who love children, earnestly request the spiritual authorities of the world to create a group of sacrifices, continue without ceasing, and demand that the governments of various countries lay down their butcher knives," it is ultimately exhausting the state of shedding tears and wiping tears, merely exclaiming, "Oh spirit is unclear, sending down this great evil."

Some say that "tears are a woman's weapon." It turns out that these women who are "so worried about current affairs that they cannot sleep or eat" have actually brought this magic weapon before the cruel and merciless god of war to use. Yuji in front of the tent still could not persuade the king's murderous heart to turn, let alone this petition, which is just an empty document, and throw it to the so-called "spiritual authorities" of church leaders in various countries? If all those who appeal for peace in the world were to imitate this "painstakingly" and follow after the "娘儿们" (women), then the day when true peace is realized would not know "where it will end." Because we are currently calling for peace and fighting for peace, it is by no means possible to achieve results by "begging" the spiritual authorities, but must have the following three points of understanding...

First, the reason why war is bound to erupt now

It is not that some killing star has descended, causing mankind to suffer this catastrophe, but rather the result of economic development under the current social system. Because the relations of production have become a state in which a minority of people monopolize the means of production and the vast majority of people sell their labor, they cannot escape overproduction, and therefore cannot escape economic crises, and its tide can be said to have激盪 the entire world. And from the perspective of the rulers who maintain the current system, in order to seek the elimination of economic panic, it can only come from the war of "re-dividing the world," so using the method of "requiring the governments of various countries to lay down their butcher knives" to pray for peace is tantamount to denying themselves. This way of calling for peace is either seeking a skin from a tiger, or deceiving others and deceiving oneself!

Second, the so-called "spiritual authority" of church leaders in various countries is actually the spreader of the various war-preparatory germs. On the one hand, under the protection of their crosses, they use the hypnosis of "motherland," "glory," and so on to drive people towards war. On the other hand, they use the empty words of ascension to heaven to make people withdraw from the practical activities of supporting peace, and fall into the passive self-destruction of listening to fate. It cannot be said that this group of humanitarians who cherish "benevolence" are the supplementers who destroy peace.

Third, just as cannonballs are merciless, most warmongers are also unreasonable. If you only rely on a few declarations and petitions to persuade them to "lay down their arms and return to their fields," that is more difficult than asking Zhang Fei to sing "Mao Mao Yu" (a sentimental love song). This point must be recognized, and one must not讳病疾医. The only way to oppose war is to use war to stop war. Let go of the cowardly child-like attitude, prepare the power of the people, and use the method of opposing the warmongering rulers to stop them.

It is a pity that the current "peace"-loving people do not plan this, but either recognize the thief as the father and live with the ghost, or sculpt the Buddha and worship it for self-comfort. Are there not many people now who want to use magical powers to summon the spirit of the Great Vehicle Supreme to seek its grace to save all sentient beings?

Exotic Mood 273

— Meng Jun

The moment I stepped inside, everything felt different. My listless heart began to stir. What I saw and heard was as if I had arrived in another country. If I weren't afraid that spring would be troublesome, I would definitely pursue the "spring" I was seeking here.

Someone inside already came to greet me, but I didn't understand their language, so I simply nodded and chose a seat. Then, a waiter who spoke our language approached and asked very politely, "Would you like to eat something?" My old friend Qi, who came with me, answered, "Beer, please."

Old friend Qi is an old hand at this. This was my first time with him. Although he told me beforehand:

"Just enjoy yourself, nothing else matters." But I, who don't understand the language, where do I even begin to enjoy myself? A glass filled with beer was brought before me, and I could only nod again, lift the glass, and take a sip.

My mouth was silent, but my heart was pounding

Page 20

very hard.

A woman from here walked up to me and asked in English, "Do you speak English?" Heavens! This was a solution, because I can handle English.

"Of course! Please, sit down! Have a beer?" I pulled her down to sit.

At this moment, my gaze was entirely fixed on her. I didn't lightly pass over any part of her, paying full attention from head to toe. She wore a dark-colored silk dress with a floral print and wide, six- or seven-inch sleeves. Below the hip was a large, long drape. A very wide, multicolored silk belt was tightly wrapped around her chest, and on the back, it seemed like something was stuffed inside, protruding high. I really didn't understand what this meant, why insist on wrapping this cumbersome thing. But I thought it looked good. Perhaps it's not just for looks that she wears it?

"You're so beautiful!" I could only convey my meaning in English. She smiled at me slightly, leaned closer to me, reached out, and brought the glass to my lips. I drank a large gulp.

Everything felt different, especially that fleeting facial expression. If I weren't afraid that spring would be troublesome, I would definitely pursue the "spring" I was seeking here.

"Have a sip of this?" I switched the glass to her lips.

"I can't. Get me a coffee."

A moment later, the coffee was brought.

"What's your name?"

She told me, and I tried to pronounce it, but even after four or five tries, I still couldn't remember it clearly. A long and difficult-to-pronounce name. I can only remember the first three syllables: Fijisu... the rest I've forgotten.

Never mind that, I can recognize her whole person anyway. She seemed to have guessed my thoughts, and her whole body pressed close to me. A hot kiss was waiting for me.

She taught me to sing their songs, and I tried to learn. Pronouncing her name was hard enough; of course, the song was even worse. But the strange feeling had completely taken over my heart, and everything seemed meaningful.

She pulled away from my hands, stood up, moved with light steps to where the phonograph was, opened the lid, and started playing a Japanese song. Although I didn't understand what it was about, the brisk tune set off the cheerful atmosphere in the room perfectly. She stood by the phonograph, tapping her body and twisting her waist to the music, facing me, constantly sending over charming smiles. In that instant, I felt supreme, I had triumphed.

She returned to my side with even more passionate expressions. I couldn't even bother to pay attention to my surroundings, or see if my old friend Qi was as enraptured as I was!

After we left there and got on the streetcar, old friend Qi asked me with a rather smug tone: "Not bad, right? Exotic mood."

Girlfriend 274

— Dao

It's really strange, recently I've run into many male friends, and they all ask each other if they have a girlfriend. If they do, they immediately heap endless praise on them, congratulate you repeatedly, and admire your skillful hand in successfully getting the objective. If not? Then they'll very sincerely pat you on the shoulder, tell you to put in some effort, try harder, or even promise to help you, feeling very surprised that male friends are generally so enthusiastic about pursuing girlfriends, everyone eager to find one for themselves. Open mouth girlfriend, close mouth girlfriend, as if there is nothing else matters, even introduce other's characters to you.

Perhaps it's because of their age, they're driven by strong physiological demands, emotion overriding reason, and they're unable to control themselves. This results in a kind of almost sexually frenzied behavior. I've carefully considered these situations, and while physiological pressure certainly

makes sense, there's another major reason: a misunderstanding of the concept of "girlfriend." Most people don't recognize that a girlfriend is not the same as a lover. Of course, a lover is derived from a girlfriend. But the reality isn't so simple. A girlfriend is a girlfriend, a lover is a lover. There is a clear distinction between them, and they shouldn't be considered one and the same. It's true that a lover often starts as a girlfriend, and a girlfriend can become a lover. But this isn't always the case. Some people have girlfriends all over the place. Can you say that all of their girlfriends are their lovers? Similarly, if you have girlfriends (let's assume you have quite a few), do you not have a friendship with these people, no interaction beyond friendship? This should be clear. A lover is one thing, a girlfriend is another. But many people misunderstand the term "girlfriend," and this misunderstanding leads to all sorts of laughable and tearful tragicomedies. I remember an old classmate of mine who was very close to a girlfriend, and she seemed affectionate as well. They often went to restaurants and movies together. But they never said anything about love, and the only physical contact was a handshake at parting. There was nothing else. It seemed like love but wasn't, confusing and bewildering, leaving the man restless and anxious day and night. Eventually, he bravely confessed his love to her, and she immediately turned hostile, angrily scolding him, saying that she respected his talent and knowledge and was happy to be friends, but didn't expect him to make such an absurd request. From then on, they broke off contact, and the man began to suffer from unrequited love, living a life of pain and misery. Situations like this are common. It's all your own fault, you can't blame the girlfriend's lack of affection. You just didn't see the difference between a girlfriend and a lover. But then again, many lovers grow out of a group of girlfriends. But this requires time and natural development, not force. It's best not to have a lover's expectations of a girlfriend.

Spring Miscellany 275

— Jian Wu

Hopping on the streetcar on ×× Road, the wind blowing felt warm. For the first time, I sensed the arrival of spring. Seeing purple swallows darting like shuttles past the electric poles, it felt so familiar! That faint cooing, those black wings, it brought the news of spring from the north!

A neighboring child smiled and broke off a green willow branch. I stuck it on the windowsill. Every day, I look first at the green leaves welcoming the wind. They easily evoke thoughts of leaving home. I observed the color of the trees in the neighboring garden, reflecting a thick green. I sighed, "Spring is already abundant on the branches." Occasionally passing the entrance, several modern young women stood in a row, seemingly waiting for someone. Their powdered, drawn-out eyebrows always seemed to be smiling. Their sleeves were very, very high. It turned out that they had already changed into "light gauze wings" of outer garments, which further highlighted their graceful and lithe figures. I recognized spring in their jade hands. Only they could grasp spring.

Amateur Mailbox

Both Sides Have Comfort 276

Editor,

I often see discussions about marriage in the Amateur Mailbox, but my marital problem is somewhat special. In my confusion, I have no choice but to trouble you as well. I trust that since you alleviate pain for everyone, you won't ignore me! Kind editor, please reply quickly! My heart eagerly awaits!

The facts are as follows: I have an uncle who left home at a young age to make a living in Jiangyin. Later, unfortunately, my grandparents passed away one after the other, and my uncle and

my mother did not get along, so he did not come home often. Later, he started a family in Jiang, and today he has a comfortable life, but my aunt has never had children and is already forty, so they often worry about having no descendants.

Since I understood things, I often wrote letters to comfort them, and they loved me very much. When my older sister got married (three years ago), they also returned home. In the midst of the joy, my aunt and uncle said to the crowd, "My older brother and sister-in-law only have this one son, and we only have this one nephew (me). The four of us will only rely on him in the future. When his parents marry him a wife, we will also marry him one in Jiangyin, so that both sides of our family will have comfort." At the time, everyone heard this but didn't take it seriously, just laughed for a while.

After the January 28th Incident, I had to drop out of school due to lack of funds. Later, feeling the pain of making a living, I was bored at

home, so I went to visit my aunt and uncle from afar. Once there, my aunt and uncle treated me very well. Soon after, I received a letter from a relative saying that they had found me a job and told me to go to Shanghai as soon as possible to work. In Jiang, my aunt and uncle mentioned a Miss Mou, who was very capable, and offered to be matchmakers for me. At that time, because I felt the difficulty of making a living, I said to them, "I'm still young, it's too early to talk about that!"

Last year, they sent several letters urging me to go to Jiangyin for the Lunar New Year. Because of their eagerness, I agreed. Who knew that after arriving in Jiangyin this time, they would bring up this matter again (more urgently than before)? During the New Year, they wanted me to go to her (the girl they mentioned) house to celebrate the New Year (her mother is my aunt's sister; she knew I was engaged since I was young? But she doesn't refuse because I'm engaged. She's sympathetic and wants to marry her daughter to me.) I was persuaded until I had no choice, so I agreed. On the second day of the New Year, I went to her house (my aunt and uncle went with me). When I arrived at her house, my aunt introduced me, but the girl was very natural and didn't care, and even called me "Brother." But I felt ashamed, and the word "Sister" never came out of my mouth. My aunt told me that she was very capable in handling household affairs, and also knew a little bit of how to read (because the family population is small, she doesn't go to school; she is an only child with no siblings). She is three years younger than me (I am now nineteen) and asked what I thought. However, I was very shy and just smiled without answering. But that girl, after seeing me, seemed to have known me for a long time, and her words and attitude were very natural. In my eyes, she is indeed a very good girl.

However, editor, I must also tell you that when I was very young (about five years old!), my parents arranged a marriage for me with a Miss Mou from about three miles away from home. However, I have never met her. I have asked several times, but it has never been possible, so what is that girl like? I don't know at all. In my heart, I hate her family for being too stubborn. Now I have several questions, and I beg you to answer them for me.

(1) Because of my special family relationship, can I have two wives? What crime is it legally? (The title of bigamy is inevitable)

(2) According to my choice, I am dissatisfied with the one from childhood. Can I deny it? Will it cost a lot of money to cancel the contract?

(3) After canceling the contract from childhood, what attitude and comfort should I have for my old mother? (Because my mother insists that she shouldn't be is what I expected.) If I carry it out, she might sacrifice herself for me.

(4) If I refuse the current one (from Jiangyin), my aunt and uncle's relationship with me and my parents will definitely be completely lost; their ardent hopes will also be vanished. In addition, doing so might intentionally make things difficult for my parents. (Selling half of his family property after going home, and recovering decades of rent on the fields, because the fields are all cultivated by my parents.) Or make my home not like a home. Wouldn't that be a pity? I want to take care of both sides, how should I deal with it?

Now I am standing on a dangerous cliff. If I do it poorly, it will be my lifelong pain and sorrow in the future. Sir, please release your compassionate heart and indicate everything. The matter is urgent, and I hope you will reply quickly. Best wishes, Xu Zhongjian

Answer: The editor believes that the reason why Mr. Xu has this problem is because he is only thinking about the family aspect and has not considered his personal future happiness, let alone his relationship with society. If Mr. Xu's uncle's proposal is followed and two wives are married for Mr. Xu, then not only will Mr. Xu feel the "difficulty of making a living" in the future, but also a great spiritual pain will inevitably occur. Moreover, the custom of polygamy and the concept of patriarchal lineage are customs under the feudal forces of the era when male power was superior. According to the principles of gender equality and modern ethical concepts, it is fundamentally unreasonable. Therefore, we hope for Mr. Xu's "one man, two wives."

From the perspective of social accomplishment and personal position, both should be resolutely opposed.

How should Mr. Xu deal with it? I believe that he should follow such principles: Marriage should be decided by his own will, and the choice should be based on the other party's character, mutual feelings, and, most importantly, whether they can help you develop your career, not on the opinions of the family. More importantly, you should not take a confused compromise method due to the difficulty of making a choice – one man, two wives.

Mr. Xu seems to like the marriage introduced by his uncle, so the editor believes that Mr. Xu can officially get engaged to the other party and cancel the original agreement of his parents. As for dissolving the marriage contract arranged by the parents, this mailbox often discusses that if they did not agree at the beginning and have reached legal adulthood, there is no problem in dissolving the contract. As for money, it depends on whether the other party has the right to compensation for damages and the size of the compensation. The editor cannot guess blindly.

As for the third and fourth difficulties, if Mr. Xu recognizes that "marriage is his own business, not getting married for the sake of his parents (or your uncle), I think it will not be a problem. You can explain to your parents that your marriage to the woman from Jiangyin is not to obey your uncle's orders, nor to oppose your parents. This fact is out of your own free will. In your opinion, your aunt and uncle are just matchmakers; moreover, even if you do not marry the woman from Jiangyin, you will also cancel your original marriage contract.

Of course, no matter how you explain to your mother, she may not be able to agree with you for a while, but we have a saying "Parents have two hearts, one is a loving heart, the other is a hateful heart." So if you continue to respect your parents very much in the future, and do not deliberately please your uncle, according to the editor's guess, your mother will definitely be able to understand you, and she will not sacrifice for you.
